trikoṇasthe śaktipīṭhe devīmāvāhya pūjayet | brahmaṇe 1 viṣṇave 2 īśvarāya 3   
namaḥ iti koṇatraye | sarasvatyai 1 lakṣmyai 2 umāyai 3 nama iti koṇatraye | tato   
ṣaḍaṃgaṃ pūjayet | tadvahiraṣṭa daleṣu brāhmyādayaḥ | tadvahirlokapālāḥ |   
yathāśakti japitvā visarjayet |  
  
154a)  
  
lakṣaṃ puraścaraṇaṃ | ghṛtaptutaiścaturbhirdaśāṃśo homaḥ ||   
  
evaṃ saṃsādhito maṃtraḥ ṣaṭkarma phalado bhavet |  
sthāpayenmanunānena prāṇān sarvatra deśikaḥ ||  
  
vījāṃtemavaśaṣṭānāmādaudūtyaḥ prayojayet |  
mṛtā vai vasvatā bhūyo jīvahā prāṇahā tataḥ ||  
  
ākṛṣṭāgraranā eṣā pramadāvisphuliṃginī |  
kṣetra pratigṛhītvetāḥ prāṇadūtyo navasmṛtāḥ ||  
  
pāśenavaddha ceṣṭasya śaktyā svīkṛta cetasaḥ |  
aṃkuśenāhṛtasyābhiḥ sādhyasyāsūnsamāharet ||  
  
dvādaśāṃgulamānena kṛtvā sādhyasya puttalīṃ |  
tasyāṃ prāṇātmikaṃ maṃtraṃ sa kīṭaṃ hṛdivinyaset ||  
  
niśītha samaye sādhye supte tasya hṛdaṃvuje |  
daleṣu vāyuvahnīṃdravaruṇānāmataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
īśarākṣasaśītāṃśuyamānāṃ karṇikāṃtare |  
yādon haṃsasamāyuktān bhṛṃgākārānanusmaret ||  
  
śiroviṃdusamudbhūtaṃ taṃtu saṃvaddha vigrahān |  
evaṃ sādhyahṛdaṃbhoje bhṛṃgī rūpāṃdhiyā smaret ||  
  
ātmahṛtpadmagān bhṛṃgān prasthāpyaśvātasavartmanā |  
ekaikaṃ sādhyahṛtpadmebhṛṃgamekaikamānayet ||  
  
puttalyāṃ sthāpayenmaṃtrī svacitte vā vidhānavat |  
taṃtucchedaṃ prakurvīta vahnivījena saṃyataḥ ||  
  
ākṛṣṭā sādhyabhṛdbhṛṃgā&statastaṃstaṃbhayedbhuvā |  
evamekādaṃśāvṛttiṃ kuryāt sarveṣu karmasu ||  
  
154b)  
  
asyārthaḥ |  
  
pūrvaviṃdūcchaṃtaṃtuṃ vardhānyādīn bhṛṃgīrūpeṇa prasthāpya   
sādhyahṛdisthitān prāṇānākṛṣya svahṛdayeputtalpādausthāpayet lamiti   
vījenetyuktaṃ sthāpanānaṃtaraṃ vahnivījenarephetatuṃchayediti |   
evamekādaśavāraṃ pratiprayogaṃ sādhyahṛtprāṇānākṛṣya   
svahṛdayeputtalpādauvāstaṃbhayediti rahasyaṃ ||   
  
vaśyākarṣaṇayoryādīnaruṇān staṃbhayetsudhīḥ |   
mohadveṣaṇayordhūmrān kṛṣṇān māraṇakarmaṇi ||  
  
pītānsaṃstaṃbhane dhyāyet prāṇākarṣaṇakarmaṇi ||  
  
ākṛṣṭānsādhya hṛtprāṇān sthāpayedātmano hṛdi |  
krūrakarmasu puttalyāṃ teṣāṃ sthāpanabhīritaṃ ||  
  
prāṇān sādhyasyamaṃḍūkānātmanastu bhujaṃgakān |  
saṃsmarettatra nipuṇaḥ sadā krūreṣu karmasu ||  
  
vādvagniśakravaruṇeśvara rākṣaseṃdupreteśa patralikhitairathayādivarṇaiḥ |   
viṃdvaṃtikaiḥ kṣagamahaṃ sasametasādhyaṃ prāṇātma yaṃtramatha   
varṇābhṛtaṃdharāsthaṃ | evaṃ prayogakuśalomanunānena maṃtravit | vaśayet   
sakalān devān kiṃ punaḥ pārthivān janān || prakārastvayaṃ | devadatta prāṇā iha |   
prāṇā ityuktvā puttalyāṃ prāṇānākarṣayet | yaṃ bhūtātmanetva ca   
mākarṣayāmi 1 raṃ vaivasvatātmane raktamākarṣayāmi 2 | laṃ jīvahātmātmane   
māṃsamākarṣayāmi 3 | vaṃ prāṇahātmanemedamākarṣayāmi 4 | śaṃ   
prāvṛṣyātmane snāyumākarṣayāmi 5 |  
  
155a)  
  
ṣaṃ gūthikātmane asthīnyākarṣayāmi 6 | saṃ pramodātmane   
aṃgalomānyākarṣayāmi 7 | haṃ visphuliṃgātmane medamākarṣayāmi 8 | kṣaṃ   
kṣaṃ triprahāriṇsatmane sarvadhātūnākarṣayāmi 9 | evaṃ vaśyādau voddhavyaṃ |   
vaśayāmi vidveṣayāmi mohayāmi mārayāmi ityādyūhyaṃ || atha sarveṣāṃ   
devānāmeka daivapūjākramaḥ kathyate | gurūpadeśaḥ prāptaḥ || oṃ aiṃ īṃ aṃ   
ūṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya viṣṇuryoniṃ kalpayatu tvaṣṭā rūpāṇiyāṃ | śa tu   
āsiṃca tu prajāpatirddhātāgarbhaṃ dadhātute śrīṃ aiṃ klīṃ sauḥ | oṃ namo   
nārāyaṇāya oṃ bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ tatsaviturvareṇiyaṃ bhargodevasyadhīmahi dhiyo   
yo naḥ pracodayāt hrīṃ hlaiṃ hlīṃ hlauṃ | oṃ tryaṃvakaṃ yajāmahe sugaṃdhiṃ   
puṣṭivardhanaṃ | urvārukamiva vaṃdhanānmṛtyormukṣīyamāmṛtāt klīṃ   
sahasakalaraiṃ hklāṃ hsrauḥ | kṛṣṇāya goviṃdāya gopījanavallabhāya svāhā   
pratadviṣṇustavate vīryeṇa mṛgona bhīmaḥ kucarogiriṣṭhāḥ | yasyoruṣu triṣu   
vikramaṇeṣvadhikṣiyaṃti bhuvanāni viśvāḥ | glauṃha   
sakalaraḍaiṃhasakalaraṃḍīhasakalaraṃḍau syonā   
pṛthivīnobhavānṛccharāṇiveśanī yacchānaḥ śarmaśaprathāḥ | oṃ namo   
bhagavate varāharūpāya bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ yataye bhūpatitvaṃme dehi dāpaya   
svāhā | haṃsaḥ śuciṣaṭvasuraṃtarikṣasaddhotā vediṣasaditiduronasat   
nṛṣadvarasadṛtasadvyoma sadajjāgojāṛtajā adrijāritaṃ vṛhat |  
  
155b)  
  
gaṃkapaṭala hrīṃ sahakala hrīṃ gaṇānāṃtvā gaṇapatiṃ hava |   
mahekavīkavīnāmupastavastavaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ rājaṃ brahmaṇāṃ brahmaṇasyata |   
ānaḥ śṛnbhūtibhiḥ sīdaspadanaṃ oṃ bhūḥ oṃ bhuvaḥ oṃ svaḥ oṃ mahaḥ oṃ   
janaḥ oṃ tapaḥ oṃ satyaṃ tatsaviturvareṇyaṃ bhargodevasyadhīmahyoṃ |   
jātavedasesuna vāma somamarāhī yato nidahāṃ vedaroṃ hrīṃ duṃ durgāyai namaḥ   
| jvalajvalaśūlini duṣṭagraha huṃ phaṭ svāhottiṣṭha puruṣi kiṃ   
svapiṣiṃbhayaṃme samupasthitaṃ yadiśakyamaśakyaṃ huṃ duṃ durge bhagavati   
śamaya svāhā | parṣadati durgāṇi viśvānāveva siṃdhuṃ   
duritātyagniroṃdhiyolaḥ pracodayādoṃmāyojyoti rasomṛtaṃ brahmabhūrbhuvaḥ   
svaroṃ | paropajasisyavadoṃvyoṃ ravyoṃhamuttiṣṭhaharipiṃgalalohitākṣa yakṣāya   
su kuverāya vaiśravaṇāya dhanadhānyadhipataye   
dhanadhānyasamṛddhiṃmedehidāpaya svāhā | gagalaṃrīgrīṃ namo   
mahāgaṇapataye gaṇapatyai varevaradekṣmyaiṃ | oṃ namaḥ śivāya namo   
nārāyaṇāya tryaṃvakaṃ yajāmahe sugaṃdhiṃ puṣṭivardhanaṃ |   
urvārukamivavaṃdhanānmṛtyormukṣīyamāmṛtāt sarvajanaṃmeva   
śamānayakṣipraprasādanāya namaḥ oṃ namo nārāyaṇa svāhā ||  
  
156a)  
  
ayaṃ mahāmaṃtraḥ sarvadeva sādhāraṇaḥ | āgamavaidikamayāḥ | asya   
ṛṣyādikaṃ nāsti || atha brahmaviṣṇurudrātmako maṃtraḥ ||   
  
haṃsātmakoyamayāmagnestejasādīpyamānaḥ |   
sano bhṛtyostrāyatāṃ namo brahmaṇe viśvanābhi ||  
  
rugraṃvaraṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ jvalaṃtaṃ viśvatomukhaṃ |  
nṛsiṃhabhīṣaṇaṃ bhadraṃ mṛtyumṛtyuṃ namāmyahaṃ ||  
  
tryaṃvakaṃ yajāmahe sugaṃdhiṃ puṣṭivardhanaṃ |  
urvārukamivavaṃdhanānmṛtyormukṣīyamāmṛtāt ||  
  
asya maṃtrasya vaśiṣṭa ṛṣayaḥ anuṣṭubhau chaṃdasī brahmaviṣṇurudrādevatā   
iṣṭārthe viniyogaḥ | haṃsātmakoyamugraṃ vīraṃ tryaṃvakaṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ   
1 apāmagne mahāviṣṇuṃ yajāmahe śirase svāhā 2 tejasādīpyamānaṃ jvalaṃtaṃ   
sarvatomukhaṃ sugaṃdhaṃ puṣṭiṃvardhanaṃ śikhāyai vaṣaṭ 3   
sanomṛtyostrāyatāṃ nṛsiṃhabhīṣaṇaṃbhadraṃ urvārukamiva vaṃdhanāt   
kavacāya huṃ 4 namo brahmaṇe mṛtyumṛtyuṃ mṛtyormukṣīya netratrayāya   
vauṣaṭ 5 viśvanābhirnamāmyahaṃ māmṛtāt astrāya phaṭ 6 |   
  
ityasmāt pratilomena svaramaṃtraṃ havirbhujaḥ |   
uddharet prayato bhūtvāviyatpūrvaṃ saviṃdukaṃ ||  
  
sva evamapratiṣṭaśca śriyāgaṃdhayahaṃ vadet |   
vāyuṃ ca viṃdumapyuktātaṃ vai mānadayā punaḥ ||  
  
sajñānā mṛtayā prāṇā urcārānnabha udbhavaḥ |  
  
156b)  
  
pūrvarṇāyā viśvagaṃ vidyācchaśinaṃ vyomagaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
pratiṣṭhāṃtamathoddhṛtya tayā sahakhale vadet |  
anayā prāṇamuddhṛtya yathā vaditi maṃtravit ||  
  
kṛtyāstrametattenaivaripoḥ prāṇān dhiyā haret |  
ādhārāducchitāyāstu suṣumnāṃtaragāḥ punaḥ ||  
  
kuṃḍalī vyomagā bhūtvā jvalaṃtī sarṣasaṃnibhā |  
sāvaktrāṃtaragā bhūtvā śatruṃ pratinivartyasā ||  
  
svāgāre praviśet sadyaḥ paṃcāgni samavāyake |  
saptāhāt mrīyate'rātirnātrakāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
sarṣayaṃkuṭuvaṃjaptaṃ tattailena ca lolitaṃ |  
citāgnau juhuyādūktairarddharātre ripuḥ punaḥ ||  
  
mrīyate sārdhamāsena kṛtyāstra jvālayāhataḥ |  
citāgni sakalānaṣṭau vraṇa tailayutāni ca ||  
  
ardharātre caturdaśyāṃ juhuyāt saptavārataḥ |  
mrīyaterirna saṃdehaḥ kṛtyāstra jvālayāhataḥ ||  
  
tuṣāsthibhyāṃ pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvārdhaśikhivairiṇaḥ ||  
  
samīraṇaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya vraṇatailena lohitaṃ |  
chitvā chitvājaraktena saptāhaṃ juhuyādriṣuḥ ||  
  
mrīyate nātrasaṃdehaḥ kṛtyāstra jvālayāhataḥ |  
vālukaṃ sākṣataṃ gṛhya japedayuta maṃtravit ||  
  
sādhitamapsuvikiredaṇavāyathepsitaṃ |  
tajjalaṃ dahati kṣipramāgneyāstrābhimaṃtritaṃ ||  
  
āsaptalokaṃ lokā&śca sadahenmaṃtravittamaḥ |  
sadehaṃ yaktato dhyātvā vāṃchitaṃta tryahādripuṃ ||  
  
157a)  
  
nakṣatra vṛkṣa prakṛtiṃ kṛtvānyaistaṃ samīraṇaṃ |  
tīkṣṇatailokṣitāṃ japtāṃ kṛtyāstreṇa vardakeniśi ||  
  
chitvāgataścitā vahnau hunet saptāhato mṛtaḥ |  
nakṣatravṛkṣaḥ asya sādhyasyayannakṣatraṃ tadvṛkṣaḥ ||  
  
kāraskarośayadhātrīsyāduduṃvara taruḥ punaḥ |  
jaṃvuḥkhadira kṛṣṇākhyau vaṃśapippalasaṃjñakau ||  
  
nādārohitanāmānaupalā *? śaplakṣa saṃjñakau |  
aṃvaṣṭa vilvārjunākhyavikaṃkitamahīruhāḥ ||  
  
vakulaḥ sāvaraḥ sarjovaṃjulaḥ panasārkakau |  
śamīkadaṃdhāṃmraniṃvamadhūkāṛkṣaśākhinaḥ ||  
  
caturdaśyāmathāṃgāre madhyarātre citodbhavaṃ |  
bhasmasaṃgṛhya yatnena mahiṣyājyena bhāvitaṃ ||  
  
catvāriṃśa catuḥ pūrvaṃ guṭikāstatra kārayet |  
tāścājaraktasaṃsiktāḥ pratiṣṭita samīraṇāḥ ||  
  
citākāṣṭaudhite cāgne juhuyānmrīyate ripuḥ |  
caturdaśyāṃ prayogoyaṃ munibhiḥ kathitaḥ purā ||  
  
māhiṣe paṃcagavye tu rājibhasmacitodbhavaṃ |  
nikṣipya kvāthayedhyānakālāgni sadṛśānanaṃ ||  
  
japenmanuṃ surākṣaṃ ca śoṣitaṃ varjayettadā |  
citikāṣṭena cityagnau durgāgāyaṃ hutaṃ hunet ||  
  
samūlatūlamādāya lāṃgalīṃ raktavārake |  
ajāgaṃdhī yathāvaccakarakrośanikāmapi ||  
  
markaṭīmapita ucca yathāvadayutaṃ japet |  
caturdaśyāmathāṃgāre madhyarātre gṛhāṃtare ||

158a)  
  
gabhiṣyati ripuḥ kṣipraṃ yamakṣayama saṃśayaṃ ||  
  
avagāhya suvāṇajñastādṛśaṃ viṃvagaṃ ripuṃ |  
savituḥ prayato dhyāyejjapanmaṃtraṃ ca śaktitaḥ ||  
  
śataṃ vātha śatārdhaṃ vā saptāhānmrīyate ripuḥ |  
yatra yatrasthito maṃtrī śucinyastamanustathā ||  
  
sūryodayaṃ samārabhyayāvadastaṃ gato raviḥ |  
tāvatkālaṃ manuṃjapyādvidvān saptāhamādarāt ||  
  
sannipāta jvarākrāṃto ripuḥ prāṇān vimuṃcati |  
durgāgāre manuṃ siddho varjitānna strirātrataḥ ||  
  
japedavirataṃ dhyāyan dināstrāgnihataṃ ripuṃ |  
tadayaṃ mṛtyumāyāti śatrurjvaravimohitaḥ ||  
  
bhāvaṃ yan dinavātena ripuḥ janmarkṣa saṃbhavaṃ |  
ākṛtiṃ sthāpitaṃ prānnikṣipyollodake japet ||  
  
ayutaṃ ca tryahādarvāk mṛtiṃ gacchati mohitaḥ |  
durgāyāḥ purato maṃtrī kuṃḍaṃ kṛtvā trikoṇakaṃ ||  
  
tadagrāgni vidhānena prajapitvā samāhitaḥ |  
māhiṣaṃ gomayaṃ gṛhya ajaraktāktamastravit ||  
  
tena pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhita samīraṇāṃ |  
riporjaptādināstreṇa dhyāyan vai caṃḍikāṃ punaḥ ||  
  
mahiṣorasthalasthāṃ ca śūlapiṃḍittamastakāṃ |  
nṛtyaṃtī tadurāraṃgaḥ ṣoḍaśārdhakarairyutāṃ ||  
  
hāhākārairasadriśca huṃkāreṇa hutāsuraiḥ |  
hṛtāṃ trailokya saṃhārāṃ jvālānalavirājitāṃ ||  
  
ghūrṇitā netrayugmāṃtāṃsaṃ daṣṭādharapallavāṃ |  
khaḍgakheṭaka saṃyuktāṃ kanyakābhiḥ samāvṛtāṃ ||  
  
chitvā citvā niśāmadhye kṣatajena hunet punaḥ |  
  
158b)  
  
tryahācca gacchati paraḥ paralokaṃ sa putrakaḥ ||  
  
atha brahmaṇe'nuṣṭup ||  
  
haṃsātmako yamayāmagnestejasā dīpyamānaḥ |  
sanāmṛtyostrāyatāṃ namo brahmaṇe viśvanābhiḥ ||  
  
asya prajāpati ṛṣiranuṣṭup chaṃdaḥ brahmā devatādhana putrādi siddhyarthe   
viniyogaḥ | haṃsātmako yaṃ hṛdayaṃ 1 apāmagneḥ śiraḥ 2 tejasādīpyamānaḥ   
śikhā 3 sanomṛtyostrāyatāṃ kavacaṃ 4 namo brahmaṇe netraṃ 5 viśvanābhiḥ   
astraṃ 6 dhyānaṃ |   
  
arkaughāyutasaṃkāśaṃ raktavastraṃ mahātanuṃ |  
sruk srucau cākṣamālāṃ kamaṃḍaluṃ kairdhṛtāṃ ||  
  
caturmukha mudārāṃgamālolāyatalocanaṃ |  
jaṭādharaṃ jagadyoniṃkuṃḍalābhyāṃ virājitaṃ ||  
  
hārakeyūra valayagnaiveyormibhirāvṛtaṃ |  
sarvartu kusumaiḥ śubhraiḥ sarvavarṇiralaṃkṛtaṃ ||  
  
ādyairdevarṣi siṃhaiśca sevyamānaṃ samaṃ tataḥ |  
udgiraṃtaṃ śrutīrdikṣuśākhābhedena dik kramān ||  
  
evaṃ dhyātvā japenmaṃtraṃ maṣṭottaraśataṃ punaḥ |  
  
atha pūjā |  
  
mānasika pūjānaṃtaraṃ vāhyapūjāṃ ca kuryāt |  
  
ādhārādi pīṭhaṃ saṃpūjya tadupari aṣṭadalaṃ kamalaṃ parikalpya pūrvādi dikṣu   
nityāyai 1 śraddhāyai 2 dhārāyai 3 pāvanyai 4 yogāyai 5 śikhāyai 6 dhāyinyai 7   
namaḥ iti pūjayet | tatkarṇikāyāṃ devamāvāhya mudrāḥ pradarśya gāyatryā   
arghaṃ dadyāt 1 hastābhyāmiti pādyaṃ dadyāt 2  
  
159a)  
  
hiraṇyamaṃtreṇā camanaṃ 3 mūlamaṃtreṇa madhuparkaṃ 4 dhruvāsutveti   
snānaṃ 5 yuvastrāṇīti vastraṃ 6 haṃsa dṛṣaditi yajñopavītaṃ 7 vyāhṛtyā   
bhūṣaṇāni 8 gaṃdhadvāreṇeti gaṃdhaṃ puṣpāṇi ca 9 pauruṣeṇa srutiṃ kuryāt 10   
|| daleṣu godāya 1 pramodāya 2 haṃsāya 3 sāmagāya 4 satyalakṣaṇāya 5   
hiraṇyagarbhāya 6 viśvanābhaye 7 namaḥ iti pūjayet | teṣveva daleṣu śraddhāyai 1   
lakṣmyai 2 dhṛtyai 3 tuṣṭyai 4 puṣṭyai 5 medhāyai 6 sarasvatyai 7 kriyāyai 8   
namaḥ iti pūjayet | punasteṣveva | bhṛgave 1 pulastyāya 2 pulahāya 3 kratave 4   
aṃgirase 5 marīcaye 6 dakṣāya 7 atraye 8 namaḥ iti || vaśiṣṭhāya namaḥ ityagre |   
evaṃ kuṃbhākṣaśrakapustakābhītiravacchinnādhanaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ   
yāvadbhavati || iti gṛhasthānāṃ dharmārthaṃ kāmābhilāṣavataṃ | kecana   
maṃtrā atravyaktīkṛtāḥ | ebhyopyanyān jānīmaḥ tānarucaunalikhāmaḥ || ito   
mumukṣoḥ praṇavasva rūpaṃ nirūpyate | tadyathā |   
talpāducchāyodakamupaspṛśya prātaḥ prasannavadanaṃ svaguruṃ murdhni   
ciṃtayet | jñānamudrālasaṭvāhuṃ jñānadaṃ śivamādarāt | praṇavaṃ   
sthitvānābhyādi sthitaṃ brahmaviṣṇurudreśvarā   
dvādaśādgaladamṛtamayairupahārairabhyarcya   
  
159b)  
  
praṇaveccāraṇāyaikī kṛtyaparaṃ cinmayaṃ vibhāvya |  
  
svātaṃ tryānaṃda saṃpūrṇaṃ saccidānaṃdasuṃdaraṃ |  
advayaṃ paramaṃ tejo nityasasminniraṃjanaṃ ||  
  
iti japitvā oṃ itaḥ pūrvaṃ dehadharmādhikārato jāgratsvapnasuṣuptyavasthāsu   
japan karma sarvasva rūpamanusaṃdhāya aṃgāni vinyasya | ata divasa pūjāṃ   
samāpayet | punarvahirnirgatya āvaśyakaṃ vidhāyasnātvā   
savitṛmaṃḍalādvaiṣṇavatīrthaṃ āvāhayāmitvāṃ gaṃgesnānārthamihasuṃdari   
| ehigaṃge namastubhyaṃ sarvatīrtha samanvite namaḥ iti japan   
āvāhyaśuddhavasanādyalaṃkṛtāṃ dvibhujāṃjale saṃpūjya cidrūpayātayā   
saṃpūrṇajalaṃ smṛtvā nimajya sakaladuritaṃ saṃharasaṃhareti japan mūlaṃ   
yathāśakti japitvā ucchāya śaṃkhamudrā jalenātmānamabhiṣicya tīramāgatya   
vāsaḥ paridhāyācamya praṇavena prāṇāyāma ṣaṭkaṃ vidhāya vāgādikaṃ   
nyasitvā praṇavābhimaṃtrita jalenātmānamabhyukṣya praṇaveṇārghaṃ datvā   
saṃtarpya aṣṭottaraśataṃ japitvā tadabhimaṃtritaṃ jalaṃ triḥpītvā tīrthaṃ   
visṛjyaṃ japasthānaṃ yāyāt | pādaprakṣālanaṃ vidhāyāṃtaḥ praviśya   
akārādyakṣaratrayeṇa śoṣaṇādikaṃ vidhāya śuddhasthale paṃkajaṃ   
praṇayaṃtropetaṃ viciṃtya svāsanaṃ sasakalayorapi tathaiva praṇavayaṃtrānvitaṃ   
lipi padmaṃ saṃcitya dakṣiṇenodakamādāya vāmenapidhāya praṇava   
  
160a)  
  
maṣṭavāraṃ japitvā saṃprokṣya sohamityupaviśya gurvādīn praṇamat | tathāhi   
paramaśivādyaśeṣavāraṃparyakrameṇa svagurupādāṃvujaṃ yāvattāvat   
praṇamāmīti śirasi natvā oṃ gurubhyo namaḥ | oṃ gaṇapataye | oṃ durgāyai | oṃ   
kṣaṃ kṣetrapālāya | oṃ sarasvatyai | oṃ paramātmane namaḥ iti vāmadakṣānsa   
vāmadakṣau tu purato hṛdyabhimaṃtrya | praṇavasyāṃtaryāmī   
ṛṣirvāparamātmā devatā ākārovījaṃ oṃkāraḥ śaktiḥ makāraḥ kṣetraṃ   
praṇavo vācakaḥ brahmavācyaṃ mokṣārthe viniyogaḥ | praṇavo   
brahmaputrolātavyagotraḥ 1 akārasyāṃtaryāmī ṛṣirbrahmā ṛṣirvā gāyatrī   
chaṃdaḥ 2 brahmādevatāḥ 3 pṛthivī tatvaṃ 4 ṛgvedasvarūpaṃ 5 bhūrloko 6   
gārhapatyaṃ kṣetraṃ 7 udāttaḥ svaraḥ 8 nābhiḥ sthānaṃ 9  rajoguṇaḥ 10  prātaḥ   
savanaṃ 11 bhūrvyāhṛtiḥ 12 prāṇovṛttiḥ 13 iḍānāḍī 14  jāgradavasthāṃ 15   
viśvaḥ puruṣaḥ 16 pītavarṇā 17 sṛṣṭikriyā 18 sṛṣṭyarthe viniyogaḥ ||   
oṃkārasyaṃ brahmā atrirvāyurviṣṇurvā ṛṣi 1 striṣṭup chaṃdaḥ 2 viṣṇurdevatā   
3 rudro'dhidaivataṃ 4 aṃtarikṣaṃ tatvaṃ yajurveda svarūpaṃ 5 bhuvolokaḥ 6   
anvāhārya pavanaṃ kṣetra 7 anudāttaḥ svaraḥ 8 hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ 9 satvaṃ   
guṇaḥ 10 mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ 11 bhuvovyā hṛtiḥ 12 aṣāṃvṛttiḥ 13   
piṃgalānāḍī 14 svapnāvasthā 15 taijasaḥ puruṣaḥ 16 vidvidvarṇaḥ 17 sthitikriyā   
18 sthityarthe viniyogaḥ || makārasya vāmadevo rudraḥ sūryo vā ṛṣiḥ 1   
jagatīcchaṃdaḥ 2 īśvaro devatā 3 rudro'dhidaivataṃ 4 dyaustatvaṃ 5   
sāmavedasvarūpaṃ 6 svarlokaḥ 7 āhavanīyaṃ kṣetraṃ 8 svaritaḥ svaraḥ 9   
bhrūmadhyaṃ sthānaṃ 10 tamoguṇaḥ 11 tṛtīyaṃ savanaṃ 12 kharvyāhṛtiḥ 13   
vyānovṛttiḥ 14 suṣumnā nāḍī 15 suṣuptyavallā 16   
  
160b)  
  
prājñaḥ puruṣaḥ 17 śuklovarṇaḥ 18 saṃhārakriyā 19 layārthe viniyogaḥ ||   
ardhamātrasya saṃvartakāgni ṛṣirvirāṭ chaṃdaḥ puruṣo&dhidevatā   
maruto'dhidaivataṃ somalokastatvaṃ atharvavedasvarūpaṃ sarvovarṇasturīyāvasthā   
jīvasya prāṇeśvarārthe viniyogaḥ | iti smṛtvā tato'ṃguli śodhanamantreṇa   
aṃguṣṭhādikāniṣṭhikātaṃ copadeśa krameṇa yugapadubhayakarāṃguliṣu   
vinyasya korparādyāṃgulyagrāṃtaṃ ca kṛtvā digvaṃdhanaṃ ca kurvan dikṣu   
lokapālā&stadāśrayaṃ prākāratrayaṃ kuryāt | tathāhi oṃ aṃ oṃ namaḥ 1 uṃ   
ūṃ ūṃ namaḥ 2 oṃ maṃ oṃ namaḥ 3 evaṃ pādādi mastakāṃtaṃ vyāpya   
sthūlasūkṣma suṣuptyātmakaṃ virāṭ hiraṇyagarbha jñānātmakaṃ samagnau   
vilīnaṃ dyātvā tadabhimāninyātmani cidrūpa saṃharaṇa praṇavaṃ japet | japenaiva   
jñānāvāptirbhavati | yadi vāhyapūjāṃkattumicchati tadā evaṃ kuryāt ||   
praṇavasya prajāpati ṛṣirdaivī gāyatrī chaṃdaḥ paramātmā devatā   
jñānaprāptyarthe viniyogaḥ | aṃ oṃ āṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ 1 iṃ ṛṃ iṃ śiraḥ   
2 uṃ ūṃ ṛṃ śikhāyai vaṣaṭ 3 eṃ oṃ aiṃ kavacāya huṃ uṃ ūṃ aṃ   
netrābhyāṃ vauṣaṭ 5 a uṃ aḥ astrāya phaṭ oṃ bhūḥ ityādi   
ṣaḍbhirvyāhṛtibhirvā | dhyānaṃ | viṣṇuṃ bhāsvatkirīṭāṃgadavalayagadā   
kalpahārodarāṃhni śreṇībhūṣaṃ sa vakṣomaṇimakara mahākuṃḍalā   
maṃḍitāgraṃ | hastodyaccakraśaṃkhāṃvujā damabhalaṃpītakauśeyabhāsāvidyo   
tadbhāsamudyaddina karasadṛśaṃ padmasaṃsthaṃ namāmi ||  
  
161a)  
  
evaṃ dhyātvā vimalādi śaktiyukte pīṭhe devamātmānaṃ māvāhya   
vījātmaikavudhyā pūjayet |   
pṛthivyādyātmakagaṃdhāmādikamupasaṃhāravuddhyātasmin samarpayet |   
aṃgaiḥ prathamāvaraṇaṃ | vāsudevāya 1 saṃkarṣaṇāya 2 pradyumnāya 3   
aniruddhaya 4 namaḥ iti dikṣu | sphaṭika suvarṇa pūrṇeṃdu   
nīlaprabhāścaturbhujāḥ śaṃkhacakragadāpaṃkajadhāriṇaḥ   
kirīṭakeyūradhāriṇāḥ pītāṃvarāśca dhyeyāḥ | śāṃtyai 1 śriyai 2 sarasvatyai 3   
ratyai 2 namaḥ iti koṇeṣu | tato lokapālāḥ pūjyāḥ | ete sarvepi tata utpannāstatraiva   
praviṣṭā iti smaret | smṛtvā svātmani saṃharet | ityeka vuddhyā pūjākāryā |   
lakṣaṃ puraścaraṇaṃ | ghṛtāktaiḥ pāyasairdaśāṃśohomaḥ | evamātmarūpaṃ   
viṣṇuṃ saṃciṃtya pūjayet | jñānamupadiśati yena paramānaṃdāvāptirbhavati ||   
  
iti śrīmadāśādityatripāṭhīsaṃgṛhīte maṃtrakoṣe nānāmaṃtrakathanaṃ nāma   
saptadaśaḥ paricchedaḥ ||   
athāgneyāstraṃ likhāmaḥ |   
  
ragnistyatāridudhuṃ siṃdhavenāsvāvinirgāduniṣadaripaṇaḥ sadaverihādanito   
yadatī rāmamaṃsomavāsusedavetajāraṃ || āgneyāstrasyamārī ca ṛṣisveṣṭup   
chaṃdaḥ jātavedognirdevatā śatruvimardanārthe viniyogaḥ | ṣaḍaṃgaṃ   
ragnistanādiridhuṃ sidhane jñānātmana hṛdayāya namaḥ 1 nāśvāvinirgādu   
śaktyai śirase svāhā 2 niṣadaripanaḥ valāyai śikhāyai vaṣaṭ 3 sadavetihādani   
tejase netratrayāya vauṣaṭ 4 toyatī rāmamasoma aiśvaryāya kavacāya huṃ 5   
navāvasusedavetajāraṃ vīryāstrāya phaṭ aṃguṣṭhāṃgulya jaṃghā sujānuno rūrū   
yugmake |   
  
161b)  
  
kadyaṃdhunābhiṣu hṛdi stanayoḥ pārśvayordvayoḥ |  
pṛṣṭhataḥ skaṃdhayormadhye vāhumūloya vāhuṣu ||  
  
prakoppare prakoṣṭeṣu maṇivaṃdhakareṣu ca |  
mukhanāsākṣi karṇeṣumastaṃ mastikamūrdhasu ||  
  
krameṇa vinyasedvarṇān vidvānastra samudbhavān ||  
  
śikhālalāṭanayanakarṇauṣṭharasanā tathā |  
sakaṃṭha vāhu hṛtkukṣikaṭi guhyorujānuṣu ||  
  
jaṃghayoḥ pādayornyasyetpadānyasya manoḥ sudhīḥ |  
dhyānamasya prayogena prayoge sphuṭī bhaviṣyati ||  
  
pūrvavajjapaktṛpti syāt juhuyāt pūrvasaṃkhyayā |  
paṃcamavyastu pakvenaṃ caruṇātasya siddhaye ||  
  
japasaṃkhyā sahasrāṇi homo tasya daśāṃśakaḥ |  
arcanaṃ pūrvavat kuryāt śaktīstu pratilomataḥ ||  
  
sarvatra deśikaḥ kuryādgāyatryā dviguṇaṃ japaḥ |  
krūrakarmaṇi kurvīta pratiloma vidhānataḥ ||  
  
śāṃtikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ karmakartavyamanulomataḥ |  
prayogakāle prajapedaṣṭaupādān vilomataḥ ||  
  
sādhito jāyate paścānmaṃtroyaṃ vidhināmunā |  
gnpādayaḥ paṃcākṣaraḥ pādo jñeyo jñāneṃdriyātmakaḥ ||  
  
dhvādyonyaḥ paṃcavarṇaśca smṛtaḥ karmeṃdriyātmakaḥ |  
svādyastṛtīyaḥ paṃcārṇaḥ paṃcabhūtamayātmakaḥ ||  
  
tyādyaḥ saptākṣaraḥ paścādadūraturakṣaraḥ |  
daḥ pūrvaḥ paṃcamaḥ pādaḥ urmirūpaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
162a)  
  
to varṇādiḥ ṣaḍvarṇaḥ ṣaṭkeśika udīritaḥ |  
so pūrvaḥ paṃcamovarṇaḥ śaṣṭādimaya īritaḥ ||  
  
sovarṇādyo'ṣṭamovarṇapaṃcārṇovacanātmakaḥ |  
evaṃ tatvasamāyogātpādallaptirudāhṛtā ||  
  
tattatpādākṣarotpannāstāvaṃto vahnidevatāḥ |  
pradhānamūrti pratimāḥ svasvavarṇodi prabhāḥ ||  
  
prajvalat keśavadanā bhīmadaṃṣṭrā bhayānakāḥ |  
devatā iṃdriyotpannāḥ urdhvadṛṣṭāya īritāḥ ||  
  
devatā bhūtapākṣaḥ stīryagvaktrāḥ samīritāḥ |  
dhātuḥ pādādarodbhūtā ubhayāna na śobhitāḥ ||  
  
urmijāstūrdhvavadanāḥ keśocchāstiyaṃgānanāḥ |  
etāḥ sarvāḥ smṛtāḥ klīvāḥ iti pāthodbhavāḥ striyaḥ ||  
  
adhastiryaṅmukhopetārdharitā varṇadevatāḥ |  
ābhimukhyaḥ smṛtaḥ saumye parāṅmukhā'nyakarmaṇi ||  
  
ābhimukhyāḥ samutpannā devatā jvalitānanāḥ |  
yābhirmaṃtre dahecchatro rāṣṭraṃ sa girikānanaṃ ||  
  
astraṃ manuṣyanakṣatre dhārabheta vicakṣaraḥ |  
āsureṣu prayuṃjīta devatārāsu saṃharet ||  
  
pūrvottara trayaṃ paścādbharaṇyārdrātha rohiṇī |  
imāni mānuṣāṇyāhurnakṣatrāṇi manīṣiṇaḥ ||  
  
jyeṣṭhā śatabhiṣaṅmūladhaniṣṭhā śleṣakṛttikāḥ |  
citrāmathāviśāyāḥ syustārākṣaradevatāḥ ||  
  
aśvinī revatī puṣpa svātihasta punarvasū |  
anurādhā mṛgaśiraḥ śravaṇā devatārakāḥ ||  
  
upakrameta naṃdāsuriktāsvastraṃ visarjayet |  
bhadrā svāharaṇaṃ kuryājjayāsvatyaṃtamuttamaṃ ||  
  
upakramo bhaumavāreśa nivāre visarjayet |  
pratisaṃharaṇaṃ vāre guroḥ śukrasya vā bhavet ||  
  
162b)  
  
sthire ghurāśidhāraṃbhaśvareṣu ca visarjanaṃ |  
astrasaṃharaṇaṃ kuryāddu bhayeṣu vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
kṛṣṇapakṣanalenāstraṃ visṛjet śaśinā punaḥ |  
śuklapakṣe kramādastraṃ punarātmani saṃharet ||  
  
bhānunāmokṣa saṃhārau kuryāt pakṣadvayaṃ śudhīḥ ||  
  
paścimābhimukho bhūtvā karma sarvatra kārayet |  
nakṣatra vṛkṣe sakalānsādhyākṣān karmasaṃyutān ||  
  
tatra maṃtrākṣaropetānmaṃtrīmaṃtrārṇa saṃkhyā |  
juhuyāddīpite vahnau mārayedriyumātmanaḥ ||  
  
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīṃ samārabhya yāvat kṛṣṇacaturdaśī |  
dhattūra viṣavṛkṣākṣabhūruhoccha samīraṇān ||  
  
rājītailena saṃliptān pṛthaka patra sahasrakaṃ |  
juhuyāt saṃyato bhūtvāri puryamapuraṃ vrajet ||  
  
viṣavṛkṣaḥ kāraskaraḥ | akṣavṛkṣaḥ vibhītakaḥ | rājīrāī iti |   
  
saptarātraṃ prajuhuyāt siddhārtha snehalohitaiḥ |  
arddavastreviṣṭikālemarīcairmanunāmunā ||  
  
nigṛhyate jvareṇāriḥ pralayāddhisamenasaḥ |   
siddhārthāḥ sarṣayāṃ vṛṣṭikāle bhadrākāle ||  
  
tālapatre samālikhya śatrunāma yathāvidhi |  
āgneyāstreṇa saṃveṣṭya kuṃḍamadhyeniṣaṇya tat ||  
  
juhuyānmaricaiḥ kruddho jvarākrāṃtaḥ sa jāyate |  
  
āgneyāstreṇa veṣṭitaṃ śatrunāma tālapatre likhitvā kuṃḍamadhye khātvā   
tadupari samādhāya juhuyādityarthaḥ | tadādāyakṣipettoyeśītale sa vaśobhavet |  
  
163a)  
  
piṣṭvā yāmārgavījāni marīca madhusaṃyute |  
atyullelavaṇetoye nikṣipya kvāthayettataḥ ||  
  
lavaṇa miśritaye ṛkṣa vṛkṣa pratikṛtaiḥ |  
hṛdaye vadane nāśikāyāṃ kiṃcit saṃkṣipet ||  
  
darvyākāskarotpalayā | ṛkṣavṛkṣaḥ śatrunāma nakṣatra vṛkṣaḥ |   
tallavaṇatoyaṃ kvāthitamāgneyāstramuccaran maṃtraṃ socirājvarito bhavati |   
puttalī hṛdayādau āgneyamaṃtramuccaran kiṃcit kiṃcittoyaṃ kṣipet |  
  
kvathite'ṃbhasitaṃ kṣiptvāhanyācchatrumayatnataḥ |  
aṃbhasilavaṇāṃbhasi | saṃtapta tīkṣṇatailena saṃjaptaṃ śatroḥ pratikṛtiṃ niśi |   
  
tāpayededhite vahnau pratiloma manuṃ japan |   
jvareṇa vādhyate sadyastryahādasyamṛtirbhavet ||  
  
tīkṣṇatailena sarṣapa tailena |   
  
sāmudre lavaṇe hiṃguviṣajīrakaloḍite |   
kvathite puttalī sādhyanakṣatra tanu nirmitā ||   
  
adhovaktrāṃvu nikṣipya yaṣṭyāviṣatarūcchayā |  
tacchirastāḍanaṃ kurvan japedastraṃ vilomataḥ ||  
  
saptāhānmaraṇaṃ yāti śatrurjvaravimohitaḥ |  
sāmudre salile samudralavaṇaṃ miśritapānīye ||  
  
ādityaratha nāgeṃdragrastāgni tadviṣā hataṃ |  
vraṇatailena liptāṃ gaṃdagdhaṃ bhānumarīcibhiḥ ||  
  
adhomukhaṃ nija ripuṃ dhyātvā kathitavāriṇā |  
tarpayedbhānumālokya śatrurmṛtyupriyo bhavet ||  
  
vibhratīmuśalaṃ śūlaṃ dhyātvā durgāṃ bhayaṃkarīṃ |  
mahiṣī ghṛtasaṃtaptaiḥ pallavairviṣavṛkṣajaiḥ ||  
  
hutvā ripoḥ kṣaṇātsenāmuccāṭayati maṃtravit |  
  
163b)  
  
kāraskaraṃ vṛkṣajairdhyātvā devīṃ purā proktāṃ caturbhirmaricānvitaiḥ |   
  
ajārudhira saṃsiktairjuhuyāddivasatrayaṃ |  
ripo ruccāṭanaṃ kuryātsenāyāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
agniśūlakikāṃdevīṃ jvalaṃtīṃ pralayāgnivat |  
dhyātvā śarṣapatailāktairvījairddhattūra saṃbhavaiḥ ||  
  
hutvā vimohayecchatrūn marīcairvā sa sarṣapaiḥ |  
kālāṃjananibhāṃ durgāṃ śūlakhaḍgadharāṃ smaret ||  
  
nakṣatra vṛkṣasaṃbhūtairvījairddhattūra saṃbhavaiḥ |  
hutvā dhiyo hayecchatrūnmarīcairvā sa sarṣapaiḥ ||  
  
kālāṃjananibhāṃ durgāṃ śūlakhaḍganibhāṃ smaret |  
nakṣatravṛkṣa saṃbhūtairvraṇakṛttaila saṃbhavaiḥ ||  
  
samidvaraiḥ prajuhuyāddhanyānmāsena vairiṇāṃ |  
  
vraṇa kṛttailaṃ bhallātaka tailaṃ |   
  
siṃhādhirūḍhāṃ dhāvaṃtīṃ dhāvamānāṃ ripuṃ pratiṃ |  
śarān kārmukanirmuktān vahnijvālāmukhākulān ||  
  
muṃcaṃtīṃ saṃsmaran durgāṃ śūlakhaḍgadharāṃ smaret |  
  
tarpayedullavāriṇā |  
  
ati durgāmayomuṣṭi gadāhastāṃ viciṃtayet |  
  
mahiṣī ghṛtasaṃplutaiḥ |  
  
pulākairjuhuyānnityaṃ vibhītaka samidvaraiḥ |  
kodravairatha vā śatroḥ senāyā uccāṭanaṃ bhavet ||  
  
āturaiḥ sādhya vṛkṣakāṣṭhedhitenale |  
  
juhuyānniśi saptāhaṃ maṃtravidvaśayennṛpān |  
pāśāṃkuśadharāṃ raktāṃ viśvāṃ durgāṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
phalinī kusumaiḥ phullaiścaṃdanāṃbhaḥ samukṣitaiḥ |  
juhuyānniśiyo maṃtrī tasya viśvaṃ vaśaṃ bhavet ||  
  
phalinī priyaṃguḥ ||  
  
164a)  
  
śaraccaṃdranibhāṃdevīṃ vigalat paramāmṛtāṃ |  
pāśāṃkuśadharāṃ jñātvā siṃdhudurgāṃ samidvaraiḥ ||  
  
tasairmadhurā siktairjuhuyāt vṛṣṭi siddhaye |  
kapālaṃ triśikhaṃ pāśamaṃkuśaṃ vibhratīṃ karaiḥ ||  
  
japākusumasaṃkāśāmagni durgāṃ viciṃtayet |  
hutvā lavaṇapunnalpā madhuratraya yuktayā ||  
  
ākarṣitadvākṣitān sarvyāmaṃtravinnātrasaṃśayaḥ |  
madhuratrayaṃ ghṛtaśarkarā madhūni | atidurgeyamatpādyāḥ | ṣaḍaṃgā&   
striṣu vīriṇāṃtādurvāṇāṃ tāpyagādyāṃgāni durgā prakīrtitā |   
  
viśvādyānyakṣarāṃtāsā viśvadurgā prakīrtitā |  
siṃdhvyādyāsātakārāṃtā siṃdhu durgā prakīrtitā ||  
  
tyannāmāgnyādikāmenāmagni durgā prakīrtitā |  
aṃgaṇesthaṃḍilaṃ kṛtvā sugaṃdhi kusumādibhiḥ ||  
  
devīmabhyarcayennityaṃ prāgukte naiva vartmanā |  
atiṣaditi akṣarātmakamati durgāstraṃ nāma ||  
  
agnitya iti agnidurgāstraṃ |  
  
āharedrāvitriṣuvaliṃ caturṇāṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ |  
kṛtvā rogagrahādrohaṃ bhītāsannāpayedayaṃ ||  
  
yathāvadagnimārādhyagaṃdhaiḥ puṣpairmanoharaiḥ |  
sthitvā tasyāgrato maṃtrī japenmaṃtramananpadhīḥ ||  
  
japoyaṃ sarvasiddhiḥ syānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā |  
lavaṇairmadhurāsiktairjuhuyāt paścimāmukhaḥ ||  
  
maṃtrārṇa saṃkhyayā maṃtrī ripūnātmavaśaṃ nayet |  
śālīḥ prakṣālya saṃśodhya śuddhān kurvīta taṃḍulān ||  
  
japitvā paṃcagavyeṣu saṃskṛte havyavāhane |  
caruṃ pecejjapanmaṃtraṃ mavatī ye punaḥ sudhīḥ ||  
  
164b)  
  
arcayitvā viśadadhīḥ devīmagnau yathā purā |  
juhuyācca ruṇānena sājyenāṣṭa sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
pātre saṃpātanaṃ kurvansādhyaṃ tatprāśayet punaḥ |  
śiṣṭānnaṃ nikhanet dvāri saṃpātaṃ prāṃgaṇāṃtare ||  
  
kṛtyārogāvinśyaṃti sahabhūtādyupadravaiḥ |  
parairutpāditā kṛtyāyuḥ snānena ca bhakṣayet ||  
  
vrīhibhirhaviṣākṣīraiḥ payovṛkṣa samidvaraiḥ |  
ājyairmadhuratrayopetairetairdaśaśataṃ pṛthak ||  
  
juhuyāt saṃpadāṃ bhūmiḥ sādhako bhavati dhruvaṃ |  
bhāskare meṣarāśisthe maṃtrajñānuguṇedine ||  
  
nadyāṃ sāgaragāminyāṃ satataṃ puṣkarāṃbhasi |  
uddhṛtpādau ca sikatāḥ saṃśodhya pariśoṣayet ||  
  
nyasyatāḥ paṃcagavyeṣu saṃskṛte havyavāhane |  
bharjjayenmanunā siddhyaidarvyā brahmatarūcchayā ||  
  
siṃhameṣa dhanusthe'rke kṛṣṇapakṣe'ṣṭamītithau |  
viśākhā kṛttikāmūla hastottaramaghāstathā ||  
  
rohiṇyāṃ śravaṇe vārau maṃdavākyati daivatau |  
vihāyānyeṣu kurvīta sikatāsthāpanaṃ sudhīḥ ||  
  
gṛhagrāmādi rāṣṭrāṇāṃ rakṣārthaṃ śikatāḥ śubhāḥ |  
prasthāḍhake ghaṭonmānāṃ madhyādiṣvavaṭeṣvimāḥ ||  
  
nava su prakṣipejjaptvā teṣu saṃpūjayet kramāt |  
madhyādi devīmastrāṇi kapālāṃtāni deśikaḥ ||  
  
cakraṃśaṃkhamasiṃkheṭaṃvāṇaṃcāpaṃtriśūlakaṃ |  
astra maṃtreṇa saṃpūjya pūjāṃte ca valiṃ haret ||  
  
nakṣatra graharāśīnāṃ lokeśānāṃ valiṃ haret |  
vihitya yatra rakṣertha vardhate tatra saṃpadaḥ ||  
  
165a)  
  
kṣudragraha mahāroga caurabhūta sarīsṛpāḥ |  
amunāvilayaṃ yāṃti vidhinā nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
ityādi vahuprakārāseti || atha dināstraṃ ||   
  
ramati durgāṇi viśvānāveva siṃdhuṃduritātyagniḥ jātavedase   
sṛnakāmasomamarātī yato nidahāti vedasanaḥ parṣataraṃ || ṛṣyādikaṃ   
pūrvoktaṃ | agnistyatāriṃdudhuṃśirāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ 1   
vicenāśvānirgādurīṃ śirase svāhā 2 tiṣaripaṇaḥ sarūṃ śikhāyai vaṣaṭ 3 daveti   
hādaniraiṃ kavacāya huṃ 4 toyatī rāmamasorauṃ netratrayāya voṣaṭ 5 mamā   
āsunase vṛvetajāraḥ astrāya phaṭ 6 || dhyānamagre prayogakāle vaktavyaṃ   
bhavati ||  
  
bhānu viṃvagataṃ śatruṃ madhovaktraṃ viṣāpahaṃ |  
mūlāducchitayāgrastaṃ kuṃḍalyā bhāvayansudhīḥ ||  
  
mūlādhāre kṣipatsadyaḥ prasphuratkāla pāvake |   
dināyājvājkrāṃto ripuḥ prāṇān vimuṃcati ||  
  
kālapāvaka mūlādhārāducchitāgnau dināstrena   
pravṛddhāṃgasvādhiṣṭhānagataṃ ripuṃ |   
  
paṃcavāyu susiddhena vahninādagdhavigrahaṃ |  
dhyāyanmanuṃ japet sadyaḥ sa bhavet jvaravallabhaḥ ||  
  
svādhiṣṭhānaṃ mūlādu paribhāgaḥ | paṃcavāyuḥ prāṇāpānādi | vahninā   
mūlādhārāducchitāgninā |   
  
maṇipūragataṃ śatruṃ vahninā dagdha vigrahaṃ |  
dhyāyan dināstraṃ prajapet sa mṛtyuvaśatāṃ vrajet ||  
  
maṇipūragataṃ svādhiṣṭhānāduparibhāgaṃ |  
  
vahninā pūrvoktena |   
  
anāhita gataḥ śatrurnirdagdho maṃtravairiṇā |  
  
165b)  
  
pāśena vadhvā śīghrena nīyate yama kiṃkaraiḥ ||  
  
anāhato nāmanābherūrddhabhāge vāyusthānaṃ ||  
  
viśuddhisthānago vairādinadīpitaḥ |  
  
adhomukhaḥ smṛtastūrṇaṃ parāsuḥ syāddinatrayāt |  
viśuddhisthānaṃ pūrvokta vāyusthānādu paribhāgaḥ ||  
  
nābhimātrodake sthitvā dhyāyan viṃvaṃ dineśituḥ |  
vairiṇaṃ dagdhasarvāṃgaṃ maṃtramaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ ||  
  
japet saptadinā darvāk yamalokaṃ sa gacchati |  
āravāraṃ samārabhya saptāraṃ prajapenmanuṃ ||  
  
sūryodayaṃ samārabhya yāvadastamayo bhavet |  
sannipāta jvarākrāṃto yamagrasto bhavedariḥ ||  
  
āravāraṃ bhaumavāraṃ |  
  
ājñāyāṃ nihitaṃ śatruṃ dahedastrāgninādhiyā |  
putramitra kalatrādīn hitvā mṛtyumupāśrayet ||  
  
ājñāyāmiti viśuddhisthānādu paribhāgaḥ |  
sthitvā durgālaye maṃtrī trirātraṃ varjitāśanaḥ ||  
  
dinavāreṇa viddhāṃgaṃ vairiṇaṃ praticiṃtayan |  
japenmaṃtramimaṃ śatrurjvarito maraṇaṃ vrajet ||  
  
spṛṣṭvā durgāṃ japanmaṃtraṃ manasthaṃ tridinaṃ smaran |  
śūlaprotaṃ nijaṃ ripuṃ dināstreṇa pradīpitaṃ ||  
  
jvareṇa mahatāviṣṭo jāyate sauyamātithiḥ |  
ravimaṃḍalagaṃ śatruṃ daṣṭaṃ tadravyapannagaiḥ ||  
  
viṣāgni dagdhasarvāṃgaṃ dhyāyannuṣṇena cāriṇā |  
tarpayeddina vātenasyādevīyama vallabhaḥ ||  
  
166a)  
  
raviviṃvādā gatayā jvālayāgrasta vigrahaṃ |  
ripuṃ dhyātvā japenmaṃtraṃ sa krīḍati yamāṃtike ||  
  
grahayuktārkaviṃvasthaṃ viddhaṃ maṃtramayaiḥ śaraiḥ |  
pratipadya nijaṃ śatruṃ japedayutamastravit ||  
  
ripuṃ na yati śīghreṇa yamadūto yamālayaṃ |  
  
grahayukte rāhugrastaṃ ||  
  
pralayānalasaṃkāśāṃ kālarātrimivāparaṃ |  
śūlapāśadharāṃdevīṃ siṃhaskaṃdhaniṣeḍuṣīṃ ||  
  
sa viturmaṃḍalādhasthāṃ raktanetratrayodgataiḥ |  
visphuliṃgairnirdahaṃtīṃ ripumākulavigrahaṃ ||  
  
spaṣṭa daṃṣṭrādharāṃ nṛtyadbhṛkuṭī bhīṣaṇānanāṃ |  
darśayaṃtīṃ nijaṃ śatruṃ tarjanyā bhīmarūpayā ||  
  
daṃṣṭrāma yūṣajālena dyotayaṃtīṃ digaṃtaraṃ |  
śūlena vairiṇo vakṣo dārayaṃtīṃ bhayaṃkarīṃ ||  
  
japeddina trayaṃ maṃtramārayed ripu mātmanaḥ |  
astramaṃtrakṛta nyāsaḥ pralayāgni samaprabhāṃ ||  
  
raktavastradharāṃ kruddhāṃ raktanetra trayānvitāṃ |  
siṃhādhirūḍhāṃ dhāvaṃtīṃ dhāvamānāṃ ripuṃ prati ||  
  
khaḍgena tacchiraśchitvā kṣaṇādvyomasthalaṃgatāṃ |  
dhyātvā durgāṃ japanmaṃtrī tridinaṃ varjitāśanaḥ ||  
  
anenaiva vidhānena ripurmṛtyu priyo bhavet |  
karmāṇyetāni kurvīta divasena tu rātriṣu ||  
  
paścimāmukhaliṃgasya sa vījaṃ mahiṣaṃ puraḥ |  
nikhanettasya śirasi kuṃḍaṃ kṛtvā trikoṇakaṃ ||  
  
166b)  
  
tasmin samedhite vahnau yathāvaddeśikottamaḥ |  
sādhakonāma maṃtrāṇāṃ sādhyanāma samanvitaṃ ||  
  
ajāraktena saṃsiktān kāraskarasamidvarān |  
sahasraṃ juhuyāddevīṃ dhyātvā savitrimaṃḍale ||  
  
pralayāgni samāṃghorāṃ dvātriṃśaḍbhujaśobhitāṃ |  
udyadāyudha saṃyuktāṃ nṛtyaṃtīṃ siṃhamastake ||  
  
mahādaṃṣṭrāṃ mahābhīmāṃ jvalatkeśīṃ tadunmukhīṃ |  
raktānna māṃsavadanāṃ ghūrṇitāgra vilocanāṃ ||  
  
anena vidhinā śatrurmahājvaranipīḍitaḥ |  
vimuṃcati nijaṃ dehaṃ putramitra kalatrakaiḥ ||  
  
ūrdhvamuktāṃbhaso maṃtrī laṃvayitvā bhujaṃgamaṃ |  
bhānuviṃvagatāṃ durgāṃ sahasrādityasannibhāṃ ||  
  
sahasrapāṇi caraṇāṃ sahasrākṣi śiromukhīṃ |  
sahasranāgavaddhāṃgīṃ trāsayaṃtīṃ jagattrayīṃ ||  
  
dhyāyannanena sarpāspetarpayedullavāriṇā |  
saṃyataḥ kālapāśena vairī mucyeta jīvitaṃ ||  
  
madhyāhnārkāyutaprakhyāṃ na daṃtīṃ narasiṃhavat |  
ghorasiṃha samāsīnāṃ mahābhīṣaṇa darśanāṃ ||  
  
śūlaprotā hitāṃ dhyāyan japenmaṃtramananyadhīḥ |  
tarpayedullatoyena sarpavaktre dinatrayaṃ ||  
  
yamasya bhuvanaṃ gaccheda rātirnātra saṃśayaḥ |  
ṛkṣavṛkṣa pratikṛtiṃ pratiṣṭhita samīraṇāṃ ||  
  
ullodake vinikṣipya viṣāde vidhinā tataḥ |  
arkeṃdvana na saṃkāśāṃ khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
167a)  
  
nayana trayasaṃgacchadvisphuliṃgaśatākulāṃ |  
siṃhasthāṃ sarpabhūṣāḍhyāṃ trailokya bhayadāyinīṃ ||  
  
khaḍgaktattāhitaṃ dhyāyan prajapeda yutaṃ manuṃ |  
vidhānenāmunā śatrurgrasto bhavati mṛtyunā ||  
  
prakalpya durgāyatane trikoṇaṃ kuṃḍamuttamaṃ |  
tatra saṃjvalite vahnau mahiṣīśaṃskṛtā kṛtāṃ ||  
  
puttalīmajaraktāktāṃ pratiṣṭhita samīraṇāṃ |  
chitvā chitvā prajuhuyādajaraktānvitāṃ niśi ||  
  
dhyātvā durgāṃ pranṛtyaṃtīṃ mahiṣorasthalāṃtare |  
śūlena mahiṣasyāṃgaṃbhiṃdaṃtīṃ ghoradarśanāṃ ||  
  
aṭṭahāsai rajasrocchairbhīṣitāṃ surasevitāṃ |  
pralayānalasaṃkāśāṃ bhramannetratrayānvitāṃ ||  
  
saṃdaṣṭādharasaṃbhinnāṃ daṃṣṭrā bhīmamukhāṃvujāṃ |  
khaḍgakheṭakayuktāṃktiḥ kanyakābhiḥ samāvṛtāṃ ||  
  
anena vidhinā śatruḥ prayāti yamasaṃnidhiṃ |  
dināstrametatkathitaṃ śatrunigrahakāraṇaṃ ||  
  
atha kṛtyāstraṃ |   
  
raṃdaṣadaripanaḥ sadavetihādaniyato yatoyatī rāmamasedhavāna   
sudavedravetajāgnista nāridudhuṃsiṃdavenākhā vinirgādu araṃ | etat krameṇa   
ṣaḍaṃgāni || atha prayogaḥ |   
  
kṛtāstra coditān kuryāt prayogān maṃtravittamaḥ |   
ādhārāducchitāṃ devīṃ kuṃḍalī sarparūpiṇīṃ ||  
  
167b)  
  
suṣumṇā raṃdhramārgeṇa jātaṃ vyomasthalaṃ tataḥ |  
mukhena śatrumādāya nivṛttāṃ svagṛhaṃ prati ||  
  
jvalaṃ jvālānalādīptāṃ viciṃtya prajapenmanuṃ |  
saptabhirvāsaraiḥ śatrurmṛtyumāpnoti mohitaḥ ||  
  
aṃgāravāre cityagnau sarṣapa snehalohitaṃ |  
siddhārthaṃ kuḍavaṃ japtaṃ juhuyāt pakṣamātrataḥ ||  
  
kṛtyāstra jvālayā dagdho ripuryamapuraṃ vrajet |  
caturdaśyā mardharātre citāsthīnyaṣṭa sādhakaḥ ||  
  
vraṇataila viliptāni citāgnau juhuyāttataḥ |  
anena vidhinā śatrurmṛtyumāpnoti kātaraḥ ||  
  
tuṣāsthi nirmitāṃ śatrorvraṇatailapariplutāṃ |  
pratimāṃ sthāpita prāṇāṃ juhuyānniśikārakaḥ ||  
  
chitvā chitvā jaraktena saptāhān mrīyate ripuḥ |  
śmaśāna vālukāṃ spṛṣṭvā sākṣānniśiṣutāṃ japet ||  
  
vikirettāstaḍāgādau kṛtyāstra kvathitaṃ jalaṃ |  
tadāyaṃ pītamacirānnihaṃti sakalān janān ||  
  
kṛṣṇāṃgāra caturdaśyāṃ prajaptaiḥ pretabhasmabhiḥ |  
mahiṣājyena lulitāstanmaṃtrākṣara saṃkhyayā ||  
  
nirmitāṃ gulikā etāḥ samyak japtasamīraṇā |  
nitākāṣṭodhite vahnau juhuyāt dṛḍhamānasaḥ ||  
  
caturdaśī trayā darvāk śatrurmṛtyu priyo bhavet |  
śmaśāna bhasma siddhārthaṃ paṃcagavye vinikṣipet ||  
  
168a)  
  
mahiṣe saṃsmaran devīṃ kālāgni sadṛśa prabhāṃ |  
bharjayet praṃjapan maṃtraṃ citākāṣṭedhitegnale ||  
  
durgāgāre prajuhuyādane nāyuta mastravit |  
punarādāya tadbhasma senāyāṃ vairiṇaḥ kṣipet ||  
  
sā senā vahudhā bhinnā jvararoga vimohitā |  
āyudhāni parityajya yuddhakāle palāyate ||  
  
viṣakāṣṭāṃkāraskarakāṣṭāṃ ||  
  
gehe dāmādikaṃ kṣiptaṃ kuryāduccāṭanaṃ kṣaṇāt |  
saptavāreṣu gulikā durgā veśmasuṃśarkarāḥ ||  
  
japtamāheṃdra digvajra gṛhītvā prajapanmanuṃ |  
caturdaśyāṃ riporgehe nikhanet prajapanmanuṃ ||  
  
siddhaṃ putrakalatrādyaiḥ |  
  
mahiṣī paṃcagavyeṣu bharjayettāṃ yathā purā |  
bhūyo japitvā vikire gehagrāmapureṣvimāḥ ||  
  
sa deśo naśyati kṣipraṃ dagdhomaṃtra bhavāgninā |  
brahmadaṃḍī markaṭikā krayakrāśanikātrayaṃ ||  
  
bhaumavāresu kulike gṛhītvā prajapanmanuṃ |  
caturdaśyāṃ riporgehe nikhanet prajapanmanuṃ ||  
  
sārdhaṃ putrakalatrādyai runmādo jāyate ripoḥ |  
  
brahmadaṃḍī markaṭi kākavacchu |  
  
ekaikaṃ vā japenmaṃtraṃ maṃḍalāt saphalaṃ bhavet |  
ṣaḍviṃdu ṣaṭkaṃ puttalyāṃ nikhanedodanānvitāṃ ||  
  
spṛṣṭvā tāṃ prajapedastraṃ kṛṣṇāṣṭāmyāṃ niśārdhataḥ |  
śatrornāma samāyuktāṃ śmaśāne nikhanedimaṃ ||  
  
praṇaśpetā ripuḥ śīghraṃ sa kuṭuṃvaḥ sa vāṃdhavaḥ |  
  
168b)  
  
ṣaḍviṃdu ṣaṭkaṃ ṣaḍviṃduḥ kīṭaka viśeṣaḥ ||  
  
kapāla sakalānmaṃtrī kṛtyāṃstrākṣara saṃkhyakān |  
saṃspṛśya prajapedastraṃ prāṇasthāpana pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
kṛṣṇavāre caturdaśyāṃ śmaśāne viṣavṛkṣake |  
juhuyāda jaraktāktān kṛtyāstra jvālayāhataḥ ||  
  
ripuryamapuraṃ gacchen mahājvaravimohitaḥ |  
  
kapāla sakalān prāṇi śiraḥ khaṃḍān |  
  
ajaraktena saṃpūrṇe kalaśe nikṣipe dahiṃ |  
kapālenapidhāyainaṃ chādayedrakta vāsasā ||  
  
pūjayed rakta puṣpādyaiḥ spṛṣṭvā tama yutaṃ japet |  
bhaumavāre niśāmadhye kāraskara samanvite ||  
  
śmaśānaṃ vahnau juhuyād gacched yamapuraṃ ripuḥ |  
sādhyanakṣatra vṛkṣeṇa kṛtvā kuṃbhaṃ prapūrayet ||  
  
māhiṣaiḥ paṃcagavyaistaṃ viḍālaṃ tatra nikṣipet |  
japapūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ samācaret ||  
  
kāraskara bhave vahnau kṛtyāstreṇa samedhite |  
ayutaṃ vraṇatailena hutvānnaitaṃ ghaṭaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
āmastakaṃ samuddhṛtya japenmaṃtra mananyadhīḥ |  
juhuyādvinipātena tridinānmrīyate ripuḥ ||  
  
viḍālo mārjāraḥ |  
  
vraṇatailaṃ bhallātakatailaṃ |  
  
suṃdaraṃ mahiṣī vatsamekarātramupoṣitaṃ |  
pāyagnenmahiṣīsarpiḥ prasthaṃ maṃtreṇa maṃtravit ||  
  
kuśairāvaddha sarvāṃgaṃ sthāpita prāṇamaṃjasā |  
kāraskaredhite vahnau vraṇatailena maṃtravit ||  
  
homaṃ kṛtvā yutaṃ vatsa juhuyādvatamānasaḥ |  
ekena divase nārirgacchedyamapuraṃ sukhī ||  
  
trikoṇa kuṃḍa nihite vahnau maṃtre dīpite |  
  
169a)  
  
arcite gaṃdhpuṣpādyaira yutaṃ juhuyāt kramāt ||  
  
rājī bhallātaka tilatilaiḥ saptadinaṃ tataḥ |  
prasūtisamayaprāptāṃ mahiṣīṃ sthāpitaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
pūjitāṃ gaṃdhapuṣpādyaiḥ spṛśan kūrcenatāṃ japan |  
mastakādyoniparyaṃtaṃ vidhau vatsamanusmaran ||  
  
ākṛṣ *? hastapatitaṃ juhuyādedhite'nale |  
evaṃ kṛte samutpannā kṛtyā dīptāṃdutāśanāt ||  
  
bhakṣayeda cirācchatrumīśvareṇāpi rakṣitaṃ |  
punaragnau viśatyeṣākartāramapikāṃkṣati ||  
  
evaṃ vidhāni karmāṇayaḥ kuryānmaṃtravittamaḥ |  
sa japedātma rakṣārthe maṃtraṃ mṛtyuṃjayādikaṃ ||  
  
iti śrīmadāśādityatripāṭhisaṃgṛhīte maṃtrakoṣe astrādimaṃtrakathanaṃ   
nāmāṣṭādaśaḥ paricchedaḥ ||  
atha yaṃtre vaktavye pūrvaṃ homīyadravyaparibhāṣā likhyate ||   
  
atha tu homadravyāṇāṃ paribhāṣā vidhīyate |  
karṣamātraṃ ghṛtaṃ home śuktimātraṃ payaḥ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
uktāni paṃcagavyāni tatsamāni manīṣibhiḥ |  
tatsamaṃ madhudugdhānnamakṣimātramudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
dadhiprasṛtimātraṃ syāllājāḥ syurmuṣṭi saṃmitāḥ |  
pṛthukāstatpramāṇāḥ syuḥ saktavastu tathoditāḥ ||  
  
guḍaṃ palārdhamānaṃ syādikṣuḥ parvāvadhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
ekaikaṃ patrapuṣpāṇi tathā pūṣāni kalpayet ||  
  
kadalīphalanāraṃgaphalānye kaikaśo viduḥ |  
mātuluṃgaṃ catuḥkhaṃḍaṃ panasaṃ daśadhā smṛtaṃ ||  
  
aṣṭadhā nāri kerāṇi khaṃḍitāni vidurvudhāḥ |  
tridhā kṛtaṃ phalaṃ vilvaṃ kapicchaṃ khaṃḍitaṃ *?dhā ||  
  
169b)  
  
urvāruka phalaṃ hyeme khaṃḍitaṃ coditaṃ tridhā |  
phalānyanyāni khaṃḍāni samidhaḥ syurdaśāṃgulaiḥ ||  
  
dṛrvātrayaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ guḍūcī caturaṃgulā |  
vrīhayo muṣṭimātrāḥ syurmudga ***? vā api ||  
  
taṃḍulāḥ syustadardhāṃśāḥ kodravyamuṣṭimaṃmitāḥ |  
tilāśculukamātrāḥ syuḥ sarṣapāstat pramāṇataḥ ||  
  
śukti pramāṇaṃ pravaṇaṃ marīcānyapi viṃśatiḥ |  
puraṃ vadaramānaṃ syādrāmaṭhaṃ tatsamaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
caṃdanā gurukarpūrakastūrī kuṃkumāni ca |  
tittilī vījamānāni samuddiṣṭāni deśikaiḥ ||  
  
iti homīya dravyāṇi ||  
  
athāgni viśeṣāḥ |   
  
vaiśvānaraṃ sthitaṃ dhyāye samiddhomeṣu sarvadā |   
śayānamājya homeṣu niṣaṇaṃ śeṣavastuṣu ||  
  
āsyāṃtarjuhuyādagnervipaścit sarvakarmasu |  
karṇahome bhavedvyādhirnetre'ṃdhatvamudīritaṃ ||  
  
nāśikāyāṃ manaḥ pīḍāmastake dhanasaṃkṣayaḥ |  
svarṇasiṃdūravālārkakuṃkumakṣodasannibhaḥ ||  
  
suvarṇa tejasovarṇaḥ śobhanaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |  
bherīvāridahastīṃdradhvanirvahneḥ śubhāvahaḥ ||   
  
nāgacaṃpaka punnāgapāṭalā yūthikānibhaḥ |  
padmeṃdīvarakahlārasāryarguggulasannibhaḥ ||  
  
yāvakasya śubhogaṃdhaḥ ityuktastaṃtravedibhiḥ |  
pradakṣiṇāstyaktakaṃpāḥ chatrābhāḥ śikhinaḥ śikhāḥ ||  
  
170a)  
  
śubhadā japamānasya rāṣṭrasyāpi viśeṣataḥ |  
kuṃdeṃdu dhavalo dhūmo vahneḥ proktaḥ śubhāvahaḥ ||  
  
kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇagate varṇo japamānaṃ vināśayet |  
svato rājyaṃ nihaṃtyāśu vāyasasya tu sannibhaḥ ||  
  
kharasvarasamo vahnerdhvaniḥ sarvavināśakṛt |  
pūtigaṃdho hutabhujo hoturduḥkhaprado bhavet ||  
  
chinnāvṛttā śikhā kuryānmṛtyurdhana parikṣayaṃ |  
śukapakṣa nibho dhūmaḥ pītavāsa samaprabhaḥ ||  
  
hāniṃ tu ragajātīnāṃgavāṃ ca kurute'cirāt |  
evaṃvidheṣu doṣeṣu prāyaścittāya deśikaḥ ||  
  
mūlenājyena juhuyāt prāyaścittāya deśikaḥ |  
  
evaṃ agniṣo homo jñātavya iti || atha yaṃtrāṇi | tatra mātṛkā yaṃtraṃ ||   
tārttīyojvalakarṇikaṃ svarayugairāvirbhavat kesaraṃ sargollāsivasuchadaṃ vasumatī   
gehena saṃveṣṭitaṃ | tārādhīśvara vārivarṇa vilasaddikoṇa saṃśobhivāyaṃtraṃ   
varṇamanoḥ padaṃ nigaditaṃ sarvāmayaghnaṃ paraṃ tārttīyaṃ   
tripurāmaṃtravījaṃ sauḥ iti tṛtīyaṃ vījaṃ | anyat sugamaṃ   
tārādhīśaścaṃdrastadvījaṃ ṭamiti |   
  
170b)  
  
vārivījaṃ vamiti koṇe || trilohinī mudrā yathā ||   
  
somasūryāgni rūpāḥ syurvarṇa lohatrayaṃ matāḥ |  
raupyamiṃduḥ smṛto hemasūryastāmaṃ hutāśanaḥ ||  
  
lohabhāgāḥ samuddiṣṭāḥ svarādyakṣara saṃkhyayā |  
tairlohaiḥ kārayenmudrāṃ asaṃkalita saṃgatāṃ ||  
  
sāgraṃ sahasraṃ saṃjapya spṛṣṭvā tāṃ juhuyānnaraḥ |  
tasyāṃ saṃpātayenmaṃtrī sarpiṣā pūrvasaṃkhyayā ||  
  
niḥkṣipya kuṃbhe tāṃ mudrāṃ abhiṣekokta vartmanā |  
āvāhya pūjayeddevīmupacāraiḥ samāhitaḥ ||  
  
abhiṣicya vinītāya dadyāttāṃ mudrikāṃ guruḥ |  
iyaṃ raktā kṣudrarogaviṣajvaravināśinī ||  
  
vyālacoramṛgādibhyo rakṣāṃ kuryādviśeṣataḥ |  
yuddhe vijayamāpnoti dhārayan manujeśvaraḥ ||  
  
svarādyakṣara saṃkṣarasaṃkṣayet ṣoḍaśa paṃcaviṃśati bhāgaṃ agnyātmakaṃ   
tāmraṃ daśabhāgaṃ somātmakaṃ raupyaṃ ṣoḍaśabhāgaṃ saṃkhyayeti |   
etadvāritamudrā uktaphaladā || atha mahālakṣmī yaṃtraṃ ||   
vedādisthitasādhyanāmayugaśaḥ śrīśaktimārānvitaṃ kiṃjalkeṣu dineśapatra   
vilasatmatrākṣaraṃ tadvahiḥ | padmaṃ vyaṃjana keśaraṃ   
suralasatpadmāṣṭayugmaṃdharāviṃvābhyāṃ vaṣaḍaṃtayā tvaritayā yaṃtraṃ   
likhedveṣṭitaṃ |   
  
mahālakṣmī yaṃtramidaṃ sarvaiśvarya phalapradaṃ ||  
  
171a)  
  
sarvaduḥkhapraśamanaṃ sarvāyadvi nivāraṇaṃ |  
vahunā kimihoktena paramasmānna vidyate ||  
  
asyārthaḥ |  
  
dvādaśapatraṃ padmaṃ kṛtvā tatkarṇikāyāṃ oṃ iti vilikhya tanmadhye   
sādhyanāma śrīvījaṃ hrīṃ vījaṃ klīṃ vījaṃ iti vījatraya saṃhitaṃ likhet |   
kiṃjalkeṣu ca vījatrayaṃ guṇamaṃtreṇa veṣṭayet | dvādaśapatreṣu maṃtrākṣara   
dvādaśakaṃ tadvahiḥ ṣoḍaśapatraṃ | tatkeśareṣu yugaśo vyaṃjanāni | patreṣu   
ṣoḍaśa svarā iti | tadvahirbhūviṃva dvayaṃ vaṣaḍaṃtaṃga tvarita maṃtreṇa   
veṣṭayet | tatkoṇeṣu hakṣaumiti likhet | iti mahālakṣmī yaṃtraṃ || atha   
bhuvaneśvaryā striguṇitaṃ | śaktyānnasthiti sādhyakarma bhavanaṃ   
vahnervṛtaṃ śaktibhirapyāvītami **? rtha*daṃ yaṃtraṃ |   
bhūpuramadhyagaṃ triguṇitaṃ saubhāgyasaṃpatkaraṃ | asyārthaḥ |  
  
171b)   
  
ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vilikhya tanmadhye hrīṃ vījaṃ tanmadhye sādhyanāmasahitaṃ   
karmakathaṃ devadattaṃ rakṣa rakṣa ityādi | koṇatraye īṃ likhet | tadvahiḥ hrīṃ   
anyonyaṃ vadhnī * *? kathaṃ eṣāṃ vījānāmekaikaṃ repha   
īkārābhyāṃ pradakṣiṇī kṛtya parasparaṃ vadhnīyāt | tataḥ * *   
sūcyaṃte hari***? ikārarephāviti | tena hrīṃ hraṃ iti | ayaṃ   
makṣaḥ sāṃpradāyikaḥ | tato hari īṃ hara īṃ iti likhet athavā hrīṃ īṃ hraṃ īṃ iti   
likhedvā | tadvahiḥ paṃcadaśākṣarairvā veṣṭayet | punarbhūgṛhena veṣṭayet |   
etat triguṇita yaṃtra muktaphaladaṃ tathā likhet | iti triguṇita yaṃtraṃ || atha   
ṣaṭguṇitaṃ yaṃtraṃ bhuvaneśvaryāḥ || vījāṃtasthita sādhyanāma sarasaṃ   
mamaumaṭayā ramāmanmathairvītaṃ vahni * * * * *?   
puṭeśvākhyādya vīja trayaṃ | ātmānātmakamīśikhaṃ hariharairāvaddhagaṃḍaṃ   
vahiḥ ṣaṭ****? suvaddha siṃcilipibhirvītaṃ gṛhābhyāṃ   
bhuvaḥ | ciṃtāmaṇi nṛsiṃhābhyāṃla satkoṇamidaṃ * * * *   
  
172a)  
  
asyārthaḥ | ṣaṭkoṇe hrīṃ vījaṃ sa sādhyaṃ likhet | kathaṃ vījasya repha bhāge   
sādhyanāma | īkārabhāge sādhakanāma | ubhayormadhye ubhayormadhyekatamāḥ   
śarasauvāra paṃcakaṃ madhyavījaṃ hrīṃ vījena śrīṃ vījena klīṃ vahnivījena ca   
veṣṭayet | tadvahiḥ ṣaṭkoṇa madhye sātmakāni sānusvārāṇi likhet |   
dakṣiṇakoṇatrayetānyeva sādhyāni anusvāra sahitāni īśiṣaṃ ṣaṭkoṇa madhye   
sānusvāramīkāraṃ gaṃḍayoḥ i harihara iti | ṣaṭkoṇādvahiḥ pūrvavat ṣaṭkoṇa   
vījāni saṃvaddhānilipibhiḥ | bhūkoṇa dvayena pūrvādiṣu nṛsiṃhavījaṃ koṇeṣu   
ciṃtāmaṇiriti | iti ṣaḍguṇitaṃ yaṃtraṃ || atha tvaritā yaṃtraṃ || madhye saroje   
daśapatrayukte māyāṃ likhedvāṃchita sādhyagarbhāṃ | tārādi varṇāṃ   
daśapatra saṃsthān ṣaṭkoṇavījaṃ vasudhā purasthaṃ | athaḥ syaṣṭa eva | kṛtyā   
drohādi śamanaṃ vyālacorabhayāpahaṃ | vidhṛtaṃ tvaritā yaṃtraṃ   
viśeṣādvijayapradaṃ || iti tvaritā yaṃtraṃ || atha yaṃtrāṃtaraṃ tvaritāyāṃ eva ||   
tāre huṃ vilikhet saroja kuhare sādhyābhidhānānvitaṃ maṃtrārṇān vasu   
saṃkhyakān vasudaleṣvā likhyatadvāhyataḥ |  
  
172b)  
  
śaktyātriḥ pariveṣṭitaṃ ghaṭavṛtaṃ padmastha mabjānanaṃ yaṃtraṃ   
vaśykaraṃ grahādi bhayahṛllakṣmīpradaṃ kīrtidaṃ | ityaparaṃ tvaritā yaṃtraṃ ||   
padmaṃ bhānudalānvitaṃ pravilikhettatkarṇikāyāṃ punastāraṃ   
śaktigasādhyanāmasahitaṃ tatkesareṣu kramāt | mardinyāmanu saṃbhavān   
yugalasovarṇakān punaḥ patragān maṃtrārṇān guṇaśovidhāya vilikhedatyaṃ   
tadatte dale |  
  
mātṛkā varṇasaṃvītaṃ bhūpuradvayamadhyagaṃ |   
yaṃtraṃ viṃdhyanivāsinyāḥ proktaṃ sarvasamṛddhidaṃ ||  
  
rakṣākaraṃ viśeṣeṇa kṣudra kṛtyādi nāśanaṃ |   
rājyadaṃ bhraṣṭārājyānāṃ vaśyadaṃvaśyamicchatāṃ ||  
  
sutārthinīnāṃ sutadaṃ rogiṇāṃ rogaśāṃtidaṃ |  
vahunā kimihoktena yaṃtraṃ tatkāmadomaṇiḥ ||  
  
asyārthaḥ |  
  
mahiṣārdinyā maṃtryakṣarāṇi | aṣṭapatreṣu maṃtrārṇān yugalaśaḥ tadupari   
ṣoḍaśa daleṣu vanavāsinyāstrīṇitrīṇi akṣarāṇi likhet | iti vanavāsinī yaṃtraṃ ||   
atha tripurabhairavī yaṃtraṃ || madhyādyaṃ navayoniṣu pravilikhedvīmānivarṇāṃ   
striśo gāyatryāṣu narabjapatra vivareṣvā likhyalipyāvṛtaṃ |  
  
173a)  
  
bhūrvivadvitayena manmathayujākoṇeṣu saṃveṣṭitaṃ yaṃtraṃtrepuramīritaṃ   
tribhuvana prakṣobhakaṃ śrīpradaṃ |   
  
asmin yaṃtre samāvāhya samyak saṃpūjayettataḥ |  
japena kṛtasaṃpātaṃ lākṣālohatrayāvṛtaṃ ||  
  
vibhṛtaṃ vāhunā yaṃtraṃ yuddheṣu vijayāvahaṃ |  
vā devāgvijayaṃ kuryāt kavitvaṃ puṣkalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
āyurā rogyamitrāṇi putrapautrān vivardhayet |  
  
asyārthaḥ |  
  
navayoni cakraṃ kṛtvā uparitana īśānakoṇamārabhya yoniṣu maṃtrīvījāni trīṇi   
2 yathā kramaṃ punaḥ 2 likhet | taduparyaṣṭadalaṃ kamalaṃ kṛtvā pratyekaṃ   
triśaḥ 2 gāyatrī varṇān | tadupari vṛttaṃ kṛtvā tanmadhye mātṛkāvarṇān |   
tadupari nūpuradvayaṃ tatkoṇeṣu manmathavījaṃ likhet | etadyaṃtraṃ   
proktaphaladaṃ | iti tripurabhairavī yaṃtraṃ || atha mahāgaṇapati yaṃtraṃ || vījaṃ   
ṣaṭkoṇa madhye sphuradanalapuraṃtāragaṃdikṣu lakṣmī māyākaṃdarpa   
bhūmīstadanu rasapuṭeṣṭāṃ likhed vījaṣaṭkaṃ |  
  
173b)  
  
tatsaṃviṣṭāṃga maṃtrān vasudala kamale mūlamaṃtrasya varṇān śiṣṭān patreṣu   
vidvān vilikhatu guṇaśaścāṃtyamaṃtyepalāśe || āvītaṃ lipibhiḥ   
kramoktamavaśān pāśāṃkuśābhyāmapi kṣmā geha dvitayena veṣṭitamidaṃ   
yaṃtraṃ gaṇādhīśituḥ | lākṣākuṃkuma rocanā mṛgamadairbhūrjevare   
hemnivāsaṃ likhyābhi vahellabheta sakalaiḥ saṃprārthanīyāṃ śriyaṃ || asyārthaḥ   
||   
  
trikoṇaṃ vilikhya tanmadhye praṇavaṃ sa sādhyaṃ gaṇeśa vījasahitaṃ | tadvahiḥ   
ṣaṭkoṇaṃ trikoṇādvahiścaturdikṣu hrīṃ klīṃ glauṃ iti likhet | koṇa ṣaṭkeṣu   
praṇavādi ṣaṭvījāni likhet | koṇasaṃdhiṣṭhāṃgamaṃtrān | taduparyaṣṭadalaṃ   
padmaṃ patreṣu trayaḥ 2 maṃtravarṇān avaśiṣṭān aṃtyapatre tadvahiranuloma   
pratilomaḥ lipibhirveṣṭayet | iti mahāgaṇapati yaṃtraṃ ||  
  
174a)  
  
atha rāma yaṃtraṃ || tāraṃ likhet koṇagaṃḍeṣu paścāt kiṃjakteṣu   
svaragaṇamatho patra madhyeṣu mālā |   
  
maṃtrohyarṇā guṇamukhasitānaṣṭame maṃtravarṇān |  
daśākṣareṇa saṃveṣṭyakādi varṇaiśca bhūpure ||  
  
digvidikṣu likhedvījaṃ nārasiṃha varāhayoḥ |  
japādisādhitaṃ yaṃtraṃ svarṇapaṭṭādi nirmitaṃ ||  
  
vāhunā vidhṛtaṃ dadyādvijayaśrī parākramān |  
gaditaṃ vai rāmayaṃtra vidhānaṃ munipūjitaṃ ||  
  
koṇeṣu maṃtravarṇān | tatra saṃdhiṣṭhāṃga maṃtravarṇān tataḥ pratyekaṃ   
hṛllekhā vījaṃ kāmavījaṃ ca likhet || taduparyaṣṭadalaṃ kamalaṃ tatkesareṣu   
pratyekaṃ mālāmaṃtrasya ṣaṭ ṣaṭvarṇān aṣṭame dale paṃcavarṇān | tadupari   
daśākṣareṇa maṃtreṇa veṣṭayitvā taduparikādivarṇaiḥ paścādbhūpureṇa   
veṣṭayet | dikṣu varāhavījaṃ koṇeṣu narasiṃhavījaṃ || iti rāmayaṃtraṃ || atha   
varāhayaṃtraṃ || madhye vījaṃ sa tāraṃ dahanapurayuge cakravarṇān   
ṣaḍāśreṣṭhābhikhyaṃgāni saṃdhiṣṭhathakaraṇadale kesarastha svarāhye |   
maṃtrārṇān vedasaṃkhyān   
  
174b)  
  
dalamanulikhedaṃtamaṃtye'tha vāhye kiṃjalke kādivarṇā vikasita kamale   
ṣoḍaśāre yathāvat | maṃtrārṇān yugaśastūccaramadanagataṃ śliṣṭavarṇaṃ   
likhitvā kṣmākoṇa vījaistadanu parivṛtaṃ sādhyanāmārṇamadhyaiḥ | darvibhiḥ   
sādhyanāmārṇairmaṃtravarṇairvṛtaṃ vahiḥ |   
  
bhūviṃvenāsyakoṇeṣu bhūvījaṃ sādhyasaṃyutaṃ |   
aṣṭaśūleṣu vārāhaṃ bhūvījasahitaṃ likhet ||  
  
sārvīśavimḍugaganaṃ vījadhārāmamīritaṃ |  
rocanā gurukarpūralākṣā kuṃkumacaṃdanaiḥ ||  
  
gomayāṃbhasi saṃpiṣṭairlikhedyaṃtraṃ śubhe dine |  
lekhinya hi mamapyatha maṃtrī kāma prasiddhaye ||  
  
svarṇapaṭṭe likhedyaṃtraṃ rājyaśrī samavāptaye |  
bhūrjapatre nijeṣṭāptyai kṣaume bhūsiddhaye likhet ||  
  
japapūjādibhiḥ siddhaṃ yaṃtraṃ kuryānnijepsitaṃ |  
rāmapattana rāṣṭreṣu yaṃtrame tatsusādhitaṃ ||  
  
nikhanecchu bhavārādausāṃgaṃ dikṣu samarcayet |  
kṣudrāpa mṛtyurogādi bhūtavyālamahābhayaiḥ ||  
  
na śakyate padaṃ iṣṭuṃtaṃ deśaṃ devatā valāt |  
  
asyārthaḥ |  
  
sādhya ṣaṭkoṇādvahiścaturdalaṃ |  
koṇeṣu cakrākṣarāṇi saṃdhiṣu ṣaḍaṃgāni ||  
  
catuḥ patreṣu nārāyaṇāṣṭākṣara dvayaṃ | patreṣu vārāhamaṃtrasya   
caturaścaturaḥ | tadvāhye ṣoḍaśadalaṃ tatkeśareṣukādiśāṃtādvaṃdvaśaḥ |   
  
175a)  
  
patreṣu maṃtravarṇadvayaṃ | tadupari śravaṇa ca bhūvarāhavījaiḥ sādhyagarbhaiḥ   
| tato maṃtrārṇaiḥ | bhūviṃvena sa sādhyena kṣmāvījakoṇena veṣṭitaṃ   
aṣṭaśūlaṃ sa bhūvījaṃ likhet || iti vārāha yaṃtraṃ || atha cakraṃ yaṃtraṃ || tāraṃ   
likhedvāṃtagataṃ sa sādhyaṃ teṣveva śiṣṭaṃ manuvarṇaṣaṭkaṃ | aṃgāni   
saṃdhiṣvatha ṣoḍaśāraṃ sa ṣoḍaśārṇaṃ vasudhāpurasthaṃ | ṣaṭkoṇa madhye   
vilikhet sa sādhyaṃ tāraṃ ṣaḍasriṣvathaśiṣṭavarṇān | aṃgāni tatsaṃdhiṣu tatra   
madhye nyaseta hauṃ kṣāṃ vidhivat prajaptāṃ |   
  
japitvā kṛta saṃpātaṃ garbhiṇīnāṃ hitapradaṃ |   
abhicāra grahonmādān yaṃtrametadvināśayet ||  
  
tāramityasyārthaḥ | ṣaṭkoṇamadhye praṇavaṃ sa sādhyaṃ likhitvā   
garbheṭhakāraṃ koṇeṣu maṃtravarṇa ṣaṭkaṃ saṃdhiṣvaṃga maṃtrān |   
upariṣoḍaśapatraṃ kamalaṃ bhūpuradvayenāvṛtaṃ |   
  
175b)  
  
ṣoḍaśa daleṣu ṣoḍaśākṣara varṇāniti || athābhiṣekamāha |   
  
palāśakṣīra vṛkṣāṇāṃ tvacomalayajaṃpuraṃ |  
kuṃkumaṃ yāminīkoṣṭhaṃ vilvāpāmārga sarṣapān ||  
  
tiladūrvājavān devī tulasī yugalaṃkuśaṃ |  
lakṣmīṃ gorocanāṃ padmaṃ va cāṃgomayasaṃyutāṃ ||  
  
viṣṇukrāṃtā markayuktāṃ japanmaṃtraṃ vinikṣipet |  
paṃcagavyena saṃpūrṇe pātre tatsaṃkṛte'nale ||  
  
saṃsthāpya kvāthayet samyagyāvadbhasma bhaviṣyati |  
tadādāya japedbhūyaḥ prayutaṃ devatā dhiyā ||  
  
liṃpet sarvāṃgametena kiṃcicchirasini kṣipet |  
kṛtyā drohagrahonmādavyādhi duḥkhanivāraṇaḥ ||  
  
sarvaśatru praśamanaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ paraṃ |  
śubhadaṃ vaśyadaṃ puṃsāṃ samastāpannivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
garbhiṇī valarugnānāṃ viśeṣeṇa praśasyate |  
asmāt paratarā rakṣānāsti lokeṣu kīrtitā ||  
  
malayajaṃ caṃdanaṃ | puruṃ gugguluṃ | yāminī haridrā | devī sahadevī | lakṣmī   
vilvaṃ | etatsarvaṃ paṃcagavye pūrṇakuṃbhe kṣipet | prayutaṃ daśalakṣaṃ   
lakṣadvayaṃ vā || paṃcagavya ghṛtaprakāramāha | mustāmaṭīniśā   
vahnirelāyaṣṭi vacāvṛṣā |   
  
pāṭhāviḍaṃgaṃ maṃjiṣṭhā drākṣā dārvī sa rohiṇī |  
phalatrayaṃ cataiḥ kalkaiḥ paṃcagavyeṣu sarpiṣā ||  
  
prasthaṃ pivedyathā nyāyaṃ maṃtreṇānena sādhitaṃ |  
śāṃtidaṃ sutadaṃ strīṇāṃ bhūtapreta bhayāpahaṃ ||  
  
garbharakṣākaraṃ śuddhaṃ paramasmānna vidyate |  
mustāmopyaṃ niśā haridrā vahniścitrakamūlaṃ ||  
  
176a)  
  
yaṣṭiḥ madhu yaṣṭiḥ | rohiṇī kaṭukī | phalatrayaṃ harītakyādi | prasthaparimitaṃ   
ghṛtaṃ samyak pācayet | maṃtrasādhita muktaphaladaṃ || atha puruṣottama   
yaṃtraṃ || kāmollāsita sādhya maṃgavilasat ṣaṭkoṇametadvahiḥ gāyatrī   
guṇavaddha varṇa su dalaṃ mālāmanorakṣaraiḥ | ṣaṭsaṃkhyaiḥ sahitāṣṭa   
patrasahitaṃ kṣoṇī pureṇā vṛtaṃ koṇanyasta mano bhavena sahitaṃ yaṃtraṃ   
jaganmohanaṃ | asyārthaḥ | ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vilikhya tanmadhye kāmavījaṃ ṣaṭkoṇopari   
aṣṭadalaṃ kamalaṃ pratimaṃtraṃ kāmagāyatryā akṣaratrayaṃ 2 |   
punastaduparyaṣṭadalaṃ padmaṃ tasya prati patraṃ mālāmaṃtrākṣara ṣaṭkaṃ 2 |   
tataḥ bhūpuraṃ sā kāmavījaṃ vaśyārthaṃ dhārayet | iti puruṣottama yaṃtraṃ ||   
śūlāṃkite vahni gṛhasya yugme dhūmāvatī maṃtralikhet krameṇa | madhyādi   
koṇeṣu marudgṛhasthaṃ yaṃtraṃ hutāśā nila vahnivījaṃ |   
dāṃtośārvīśaviṃdvaṃtau vīje dhūmāvaṃtīṃ manuḥ proktaḥ śatru   
nigrahakārakaḥ viṣeṇa kanakāṃbhobhiḥ pretakarpaṭakalpitaṃ |  
  
176b)  
  
śmaśāne nikhanedetacchatrumutsādayeddhruvaṃ | asyārthaḥ | ṣaṭkoṇa   
dhūmāvatī maṃtraṃ ekaikaṃ likhet | tadvahirvāyu gṛhena veṣṭayet | tato repheṇa |   
tadvahiryakāreṇa | pretavastre dhattūrakarasena kākapakṣa lekhanyā likhitvā   
śmaśāne nikhanet | śatrūccāṭanaṃ bhavet || māmālikhyamakārakoṣṭhayugale   
koṇeṣu tasyā likhenmaṃtrajñoṅaṇanāñjakārasahitān dhūmāvatīṃ patragāṃ |   
vītaṃ gharmaṭikādināparamidaṃ vāyutrigehāvṛtaṃ yaṃtraṃ prāṃtapareta   
bhūmi nihitaṃ vidveṣaṇaṃ syāt dviṣaḥ | asyārthaḥ | aṣṭadalakamalaṃ kṛtvā   
tanmadhyemāṃkāraṃ tatkoṣṭhadvaye sādhyaṃ makāreṇa   
catuṣṭayenaṅaṇanārṇān patreṣu dhūmāvatīṃ | vahirghumuṭikādinā veṣṭayet |   
etat pretavastreṇa dhattūra karasena kākapakṣa lekhanyā likhet | śmaśāne nihitaṃ   
dveṣakaraṇaṃ |   
  
177a)  
  
ekāśīti padeṣu madhya dahane sādhyaṃ likheddhuṃ punaḥ kṣtrūṃ śrūṃ   
vrūṃñjitidiggatā su vilikhedvījān paṃktiyvatha | śiṣṭoṣvīśa niśācarādi   
vilikhetkālī manupaṃktiśastadvāhye yamavītamagni yavanāvītaṃ ca yaṃtraṃ likhet   
| likhedaṣṭaviṣāṃgāraniṃvaniryāsakajjalaiḥ |   
  
nigrahākṣamidaṃ cakraṃ kākapakṣeṇa karpaṭe |   
vibhīta vṛkṣe valmīke śmaśāne vā catuḥ pathe ||  
  
dakṣiṇasthenilemaṃtrī nikhanedartharārdhake |   
sarvathā śatruretena saptāhānmrīyate ripuḥ ||  
  
nigrahīta mahārogaiḥ patite vā bhavedasau |  
śilāyāmi * * * *? cakrame tatprakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
markaṭī viṣadaṃḍībhiḥ samālikhya madhomukhaṃ |  
yatra rātrauravānaṃ tatra bhūyāśubhaṃ bhavet ||  
  
ākhyātuṃ puramadhyataḥ smaragatāmālikhya jaṃbhābhidhāṃ vidyāṃ   
diggatapatrakeṣvatha likheddevī daleṣu smaraṃ | koṇastheṣu samānakaṃ ca hi rataḥ   
pāśāṃkuśābhyāṃ vṛtaṃ yaṃtraṃ vaśyakaraṃ grahādi bhayahṛt   
kṣudrābhicārāpahaṃ |   
  
177b)  
  
asyārthaḥ | aṣṭadalakamala madhye tuṃ vuruvījaṃ tanmadhye kāmavījaṃ tataḥ   
sā*? dikpatreṣu | jaṃbhejaṃbhini mohemohini aṃdheaṃdhini   
ruṃdheruṃdhi svāhā sarvatra || atha mṛtyuṃjayaṃ yaṃtraṃ || puṭī kṛte   
bhūmipurasya yugme māyāṃ likhenmanmatha sādhyasaṃjñāṃ | cakāra koṇena   
mahīpureṇa saṃveṣṭitaṃ kasyakaraṃ taduccaiḥ | madhye sārṇavidarbhitaṃ   
prapuṭitaṃ mṛtyuṃjayaṃ tryakṣaraiḥkṣāṃtasthaṃ nijasādhyanāma vilikhet   
kiṃjalkasaṃsthānsurān | patreṣvaṣṭāsu nāmamaṃtrapuṭitaṃ vargeṣvatho yaṃtraṃ   
padmapuṭīkṛtaṃ nigaditaṃ mṛtyuṃjayākhyaṃ paraṃ | viṣajvara   
śiroroganāśanaṃ śrījayapradaṃ | kāṃtipuṣṭipradaṃ vaśyaṃ   
sarvakamārthasādhakaṃ | asyārthaḥ | aṣṭadalakamalaṃ kṛtvā daleṣu   
svarakesaraṃ kṛtvā kamalakarṇikāyāṃ kṣakāraṃ tanmadhye mārṇavidarbhitaṃ   
sādhyanāma mṛtyuṃjaya tryakṣarapuṭitaṃ kṛtvā patreṣtaṣṭayuk   
tryakṣarapuṭitaṃ nāmalikhet | patrāṃgeṣvaṣṭavargān | aṣṭa upari padmadvayena   
puṭitaṃ yaṃtramuktaphaladaṃ || iti mṛtyuṃjaya yaṃtraṃ || oṃkāramāyādiṣu   
mekhalegni vadhūrmanuṃ vahni gṛhasya yugme | madhyādi koṇeṣu vilikhya bhūrje   
yaṃtraṃ vidadhyādripunāgahāniṃ || asyārthaḥ | vahnigehayugaṃ likhitvā |   
  
178a)  
  
madhye oṃkāraṃ koṇeṣu hrīṃ mekhale svāheti likhet ||   
  
vihāya vījaṃ nṛkāraṃ glakāraṃ tatra saṃlikhet |   
kṣakāre nāvṛtaṃ vāhye pāśāṃkuśa vṛtaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
ṭakāreṇāvṛtaṃ bhūyobhūmimaṃḍalamadhyagaṃ |  
lakārairviṃdu saṃyuktairveṣṭitaṃ tadvahiḥ kramāt ||  
  
sargāṃta mātṛkā vīja sarvaṃ vṛttena ceṣṭitaṃ |  
kaukṣaiṃya karpāṭe kḷptamiṣṭadvayaṃ ca madhyagaṃ ||  
  
senāgre nikhanede tatstaṃbhanaṃ kurute dhruvaṃ ||  
  
madhye śrīnarasiṃha vījamatha tadvāhya svarān kesarevārīdveṃduyameṃdrakeṣu   
vilikhen madhye manuṃ gāruḍaṃ | aṃtasthānmarudagni nairṛti śiveṣvālikhya   
vargāvṛtaṃ yaṃtraṃ mājibhiraṣṭibhiḥ parivṛtaṃ saṃvartakairgāruḍaṃ ||   
asyārthaḥ | aṣṭadalakamala madhye nṛsiṃhavījaṃ svarāḥ kesareṣu | paścimottara   
yāmya patreṣu madhye gāruḍamaṃtraṃ | vāyuvahni nirṛti śikhi patreṣu   
yaralavāḥ | vahirvarāhena tadvahiraṣṭabhiḥ kṣakārairveṣṭayet | etadyaṃtraṃ   
dhārayataḥ paśyataśca sarvaviṣaṃ naśyati ||   
  
178b)  
  
atha kāmayaṃtraṃ || sādhyaḥ saṃpuṭitaiḥ smarairapi vṛtaṃ kāmaṃ   
likhenmadhyataḥ paścāttārapikārapakṣaparānnāśārpi jhaṃṭīśapān |   
śūlāṣṭāṣṭa daleṣu sādhavilikhet tāṃvūlapatrodareyaṃtraṃ tanniśikhādayet   
kṛtajapaṃ vaśobhavettatrasaḥ | asyārthaḥ aṣṭapatra padmaṃ   
tāṃvūlodarelikhitvā tanmadhye kāmavījaṃ sa sādhyanāmākṣarapuṭitaiḥ   
kāmavījaistadveṣṭayet | paścādaṣṭa patreṣu pratyekaṃ vakṣyamāna vījāni vilikhet   
| kathaṃ tāraḥ oṃkāraḥ | oṃkāraḥ | khaṃ ṛṃ uṃ eṃ yaṃ aṣṭadaleṣu   
likhecchūlāni dalāgreṣu | etadyaṃtraṃ vaśyakaraṃ || atha goviṃdayaṃtraṃ || prāk   
pratyagdakṣiṇodagvividhadabhilikhet sāṣṭarekhā catuṣkaṃ koṇodyacchūla yuktaṃ   
valayugayutaṃ madhyakoṣṭhe tadaṃaḥ | ślokasyārṇān   
parastādvasudalavivare'ṣṭavarṇaṃ likhitvā tadvāhye   
dvādaśārṇestadanuparivṛtaṃ devakīputrayaṃtraṃ | likhitaṃ bhūrjapatrādau   
yaṃtrame tadyathā vidhividhṛtaṃ vāhunā nityaṃ sarvakāma phalapradaṃ |   
palāśavṛkṣaphalake likhitaṃ sādhusādhitaṃ | gosthāne nikhanede tadgavāṃ   
vṛddhiḥ prajāyate ||  
  
179a)  
  
atha lekhyadravyāṇi ||  
  
kāśmīrarocanā lākṣā mṛgebhamadacaṃdanaiḥ |  
vilikheddhemalekhanyā yaṃtrāṇyetāni deśikaḥ ||   
  
bhūmisṛṣṭaṃ vaśaspṛṣṭaṃ dagdhaṃ nirmālyasaṃgataṃ |  
vistīrṇaṃ laṃghitaṃ maṃtrī yaṃtraṃ jātu na dhārayet ||  
  
atha yaṃtrarūpāṇi dīkṣādyupayuktāni sarvatobhadranavanābhapaṃcābjāni   
maṃḍalāni likhyaṃte || sarvatobhadraṃ yathā ||   
  
caturasraṃ catuḥkoṣṭhe karṇasūtrasamanvite |  
caturṣvapi ca koṇeṣu dadyāt sūtracatuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
tataḥ koṣṭheṣu matsyāḥ syusteṣu sūtreṣu pātayet |  
ṣaṭtriṃśattānityadairmadhye likhet padmaṃ salakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
vahiḥ paṃktyā bhavet pītaṃ paṃktiyugmena vīthikāḥ |  
dvāraśobhopaśobhāśca śiṣṭābhyāṃ parikalpayet ||  
  
śāstroktavidhinā maṃtrī tataḥ padmaṃ samālikhet |  
padmakṣetrasya saṃtyajya dvādaśāṃśaṃ vahiḥ sudhīḥ ||  
  
tanmadhyaṃ vibhaje mṛttaistribhiḥ samavibhāgaśaḥ |  
ādyaṃ syāt karṇikāsthānaṃ keśarāṇāṃ dvitīyakaṃ ||  
  
tṛtīyaṃ tatra patrāṇāṃ uktāṃśena dalāgrakaṃ |  
vāhyavṛṃtāṃtarālasya mānaṃ yad vidhinā sudhīḥ ||  
  
nidhāya keśarāgreṣu paritorddhaniśākarān |  
likhitvā saṃdhisaṃsthāne tataḥ mūtrāṇi pātayet ||  
  
dalāgrāṇāṃ ca yanmāna tanmānaṃ vṛṃtamālikhet |  
tadaṃtarāle tanmadhye sūtrasyobhayataḥ sudhīḥ ||  
  
179b)  
  
prālikhed vāhyahastena dalāgrāṇi samaṃ tataḥ |  
dalamūlena yugaśaḥ kesarāṇi prakalpayet ||  
  
etat sādhāraṇaṃ proktaṃ paṃkajaṃ taṃtravedibhiḥ |  
padāni trīṇi pādārthaṃ pīṭhakoṇeṣu mārjayet ||  
  
avaśiṣṭaiḥ padairvidvān pīṭhagātrāṇi kalpayet |  
padāni vīthisaṃsthāni mārjayet paṃktyabhedataḥ ||  
  
dikṣu dvārāṇi yajet dvicatuḥkoṣṭhakaistataḥ |  
padaistribhirathaikena bhāgāḥ syurdvārapārśvataḥ ||  
  
upaśobhāḥ syurekaina tribhiḥ koṣṭhairanaṃtaraṃ |  
avaśiṣṭaiḥ padaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ koṇānāṃ syāccatuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
raṃjayet paṃcabhirvarṇairmaṃḍalaṃ tanmanoharaṃ |  
pītaṃ haridrācūrṇaṃ syācchvetaṃ taṃḍulasaṃbhavaṃ ||  
  
kusuṃbhacūrṇamaruṇaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dagdhapulākajaṃ |  
vilvādi dīpakaṃ śyāmamityuktaṃ varṇapaṃcakaṃ ||  
  
aṃgulotsedhavistārā śrīmā rekhāḥ sitāḥ śubhāḥ |  
karṇikā pītavarṇena kesarāṇyaruṇena ca ||  
  
śubhravarṇena paṃtrāṇi tatsaṃdhīḥ śyāmalena ca |  
  
180a)  
  
rajasāsaṃ japenmaṃtrī yadvā pītaiva varṇikā ||  
  
kesarāḥ pītaraktāḥ syuraruṇāni padānyapi |  
saṃdhayaḥ pītavarṇāḥ syuḥ pītenāpyasitena vā ||  
  
raṃjayet pīṭhagarbhāṇi pādāḥ syuraruṇāḥ śubhāḥ |  
gātrāṇi tasya śuklāni vīthīṣu ca catasṛṣu ||  
  
ālikhet kalpalatikā dalapuṣpaphalānvitāḥ |  
varṇārnānāvidhaiścitrāḥ sarvadṛṣṭi manoharāḥ ||  
  
dvārāṇi śvetavarṇāni śobhā raktāḥ samīritāḥ |  
upaśobhāḥ pīitavarṇāḥ koṇānyasitabhāṃsi ca ||  
  
tisrorekhā vahiḥ kāryāsitaraktā sitāḥ kramāt |  
maṃḍalaṃ sarvato bhadrame tatsādhāraṇaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
asyārthaḥ ||  
  
uktaprakāreṇa pūrvapaścimāyatā uttaradakṣiṇāyatāśca saptadaśarekhā samāḥ   
koṣṭhāḥ kāryāḥ | madhyastha ṣaḍbhiḥ koṣṭhaiḥ padmaṃ likhet | padmamadhye   
pītavarṇāni kesarāṇi aruṇāni patrāṇi śubhrāṇi patrasaṃdhayaḥ | asitā varṇāḥ |   
padmoparipaṃktyaikena pīṭhaṃ kāryaṃ | tribhistribhiḥ koṣṭhaiḥ pītādyāḥ |   
aruṇāḥ koṣṭha catuṣṭaye kāryāḥ | pīṭhoparipaṃktidvaye nānāvarṇāḥ sarvato   
vīthīkāḥ kartavyāḥ | uparipaṃktidvayamavaśiṣṭaṃ jātaṃ | tasya koṇeṣu   
pādacatuṣṭayeṣu haritaṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ koṣṭhaiḥ kāryaṃ | tatsamīpastha koṣṭha trayeṇa   
tadarddhe naiva ca pītā upaśobhāḥ kāryāḥ |   
  
180b)  
  
dvārāṇi caturbhiḥ koṣṭhaiḥ | dvābhyāṃ ca śvetavarṇāni evaṃ ca dikṣu   
voddhavyāḥ | tato maṃḍalādvahistisrorekhāḥ śvetāruṇa kṛṣṇavarṇāḥ kāryāḥ   
| evaṃ sarvato bhadramaṃḍalaṃ manoharaṃ saṃpadyate || atha   
navanābhamaṃḍalaṃ kathyate ||   
  
caturasre catuḥ ṣaṣṭhi padānyā racayet sudhīḥ |   
pādaiścaturbhiḥ padmaṃ syānmadhye tatparitaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
vīthīścatasraḥ kurvīta maṃḍalāṃtāvasānikāḥ |  
diggateṣu catuṣkeṣu padmāni ca samālikhet ||  
  
vidiggata catuḥkānibhitvāṃ ṣoḍaśadhā sudhīḥ |  
mārjayet svastikākāraṃ śvetapītāruṇāsitaiḥ ||  
  
rajobhiḥ pūrayettāni svastikānisitāditaḥ |  
prāk proktenaiva mārgeṇa śeṣamanyat samāpayet ||  
  
navanābhamidaṃ proktaṃ maṃḍalaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
asyārthaḥ |  
  
pūrvapaścimāyatānavarekhāḥ samāḥ kāryāḥ | tathottarāyatāśca navarekhāḥ   
kāryāḥ | evaṃ caturasraṃ samyak catuḥṣaṣṭikoṣṭhātmakaṃ saṃpadyate | tasya   
koṇasya koṇacatuṣṭayaṃ bhitvā ṣoḍaśadhā kāryāḥ ||   
  
181a)  
  
ṣoḍaśakoṣṭhamadhye tribhiḥ koṣṭhaiḥ ekena ca liṃgākāraṃ saṃpadyate | tathaiva   
trayamapi | evaṃ svastikaṃ koṇacatuṣṭaye kāryaṃ dikṣu koṇacatuṣṭayena   
padmacatuṣṭayaṃ kāryaṃ | madhyastha koṇacatuṣṭaye padmaikaṃ | avaśiṣṭa   
koṇapaṃktibhirvīthī catuṣṭayasīmāṃtaṃ kāryaṃ | evaṃ navanābhamaṃḍalaṃ   
bhavati || atha paṃcābjaṃ || paṃcābjaṃ maṃḍalaṃ proktametatsvastikavarjitaṃ |   
dīkṣāyāṃ devapūjārthaṃ maṃḍalānāṃ trayaṃ śubhaṃ || svastikasthāne   
koṇacatuṣṭaye varṇikāpūraṇaṃ caturasraṃ kāryaṃ | pūrvavat padmapaṃcakaṃ   
caturdikṣu madhye ca kāryaṃ | vīthyaścatasrakāryāḥ || iti   
śrīmadāsādityatripāṭhīsaṃgṛhīte maṃtrakoṣe yaṃtrakathanaṃ nāma   
ekonaviṃśaḥ paricchedaḥ ||  
atha devapūjādau upayuktā mudrā likhyaṃte |   
āvāhanādikā mudrāḥ pradarśyaṃte yathā kramāt ||  
  
yābhirviracitābhistu modaṃte maṃtra devatāḥ |  
samyak saṃpūritaiḥ puṣpaiḥ karābhyāṃ racito'ṃjaliḥ ||  
  
āvāhanākhyā kathitā mudrā deśikasaptamaiḥ || 1 || adhomukhī kṛtā saiva   
proktāsthāpana karmaṇi || 2 ||   
  
āśliṣṭa muṣṭi yugalā pronnatāṃguṣṭha yugmikā |  
sannidhāne samuddiṣṭā mudreyaṃ deśikādibhiḥ || 3 ||  
  
śrīguṣṭagarbhiṇī saiva sannirodhe samīritāḥ || 4 ||   
  
181b)  
  
devatāṃge ṣaḍaṃgānāṃ nyāsaḥ syāt sakalīkṛtaḥ || 5 ||   
  
savyahastakṛtā muṣṭidīrghādho mukhatarjanī |    
avaguṃṭhana mudreyaṃ proktā deśikasattamaiḥ || 6 ||  
  
anyonyābhi mukhāśliṣṭakaniṣṭhānāmikā punaḥ |   
tathā tarjanimadhyeyaṃ dhenumudrā prakīrtitā || 7 ||  
  
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ kuryādyathā deśikasattamaḥ || 8 ||  
  
anyonyagrathitāṃguṣṭhāḥ prasāritakarāṃguliḥ |   
mahāmudreyamuditā paramīkaraṇe vudhaiḥ ||  
  
prayojayedimā mudrā devatāyāga karmaṇi ||  
  
athākṣamālā |   
  
ādīkṣātānya yogatvā dakṣamāleti kīrtitā |  
tadvarṇa saṃkhyairmaṇibhirjapamālāṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
rudrabhūmālikāsūre japet svamano rathāt |   
padmākṣairvihitāmālā śatrūṇāṃ nāśinīmatā ||  
  
kuśagraṃthimayīmālā sarvapāpapraṇāśinī |  
putraṃ jīvaphalaiḥ proktā kurute putra saṃpadaṃ ||  
  
nirmitā rūpyamaṇibhirjapamālāsthitipradya |  
hiraṇmayairviracitā mālākāmān prayacchati ||  
  
pravālairvihitāmālā prayacchet puṣkalaṃdhanaṃ |  
saubhāgyaṃ sphāṭikī mālāmauktikairvihitāśriyaṃ ||  
  
nirmitā śaṃkhamaṇibhiḥ kurute kīrtimakṣayāṃ |  
sarvairetairviracitāmālā syānmuktayenṛṇāṃ ||  
  
atha vaśyādi proyogopayuktāni ṣaṭkarmāṇi likhyaṃte ||   
  
abhidhāsye hi taṃtre'smin samyak ṣaṭkarmalakṣaṇaṃ |   
sarvataṃtrānusāreṇa prayogaphalasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
śāṃtivaśyastaṃbhanāni dveṣaṇoccāṭane tataḥ |  
  
182a)  
  
māraṇāṃtāniśaṃsaṃti ṣaṭkarmāṇi manīṣiṇaḥ ||  
  
rogakṛtyā grahādīnāṃ nirāsaḥ śāṃtirīritā || 1 || vaśyaṃ janānāṃ sarveṣāṃ   
vidheyatvamudīritaṃ || 2 || pravṛttirodhaḥ sarveṣāṃ staṃbhanaṃ tadudāhṛtaṃ ||   
3 || snigdhānāṃ dveṣajananaṃmitho vidveṣaṇaṃ mataṃ || 4 || uccāṭanaṃ   
svadeśāderbhramaṇaṃ parikīrtitaṃ || 5 || prāṇināṃ prāṇaharaṇaṃ māraṇaṃ   
tadudāhṛtaṃ || 6 ||   
  
svadevatādi kālādīn jñātvā karmāṇi sādhayet |   
ratirvāṇī ramājyeṣṭhā durgākālī yathā kramāt ||   
  
ṣaṭkarmadevatāḥ proktāḥ karmādautāḥ prayojayet ||   
  
īśacaṃdreṃdra nirṛti vādvagnīnāṃdiśomatāḥ |  
sūryodayaṃ samārabhya ghaṭikādaśakaṃ kramāt ||  
  
ṛtavaḥ syurvasaṃtādyā ahorātraṃ dine dine |  
vasaṃtagrīṣmavarṣākhyaśaraddhe maṃtaśaiśirāḥ ||  
  
hemaṃtaḥ śāṃtike prokto vasaṃto vaśyakarmaṇi |  
śiśiraḥ staṃbhane jñeyo vidveṣo brahma īritaḥ ||  
  
prāvṛduccāṭane jñeyā śaranmāraṇa karmaṇi |  
padmākhyaṃ svastikaṃ bhūyo vikaṭaṃ kukkuṭaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
vajraprahvākhyamāhurāsanāni manīṣiṇaḥ |  
ṣaṇmudrāḥ kramato jñeyāḥ padmapāśagadādvayaḥ ||  
  
muśalāsallikhaḍgākhyāḥ śāṃtikādiṣu karmasu |  
jaleṃ śāṃtividhauśastaṃ vaśye vahnirudīritaḥ ||  
  
staṃbhane pṛthivīśastā vidveṣe vyomakīrtitaṃ |  
uccāṭane smṛto vāyu bhūyognirmāraṇe mataḥ ||  
  
tattadbhūtodake samyak tattanmaṃḍala saṃyutaṃ |  
tattatkarmavidhātavyaṃ tṛṇāni niśitātmanā ||  
  
182b)  
  
sitāṃtyusalilakṣoṇī vyomavāyuhavirbhujaḥ |  
maṃtrāṃ syurvarṇavījāni ṣaṭkarmasu yathā kramāṃ ||  
  
gaṃthanaṃ ca vidarbhaśca saṃpuṭo ropaṇaṃ tathā |  
yogaḥ pallava ityete vinyāsāḥ ṣaṭsukarmasu ||  
  
maṃtrārṇāṃtaritān kuryānnāma varṇān yathāvidhi |  
gaṃthanaṃ taddhi vijñeyaṃ praśastaṃ śāṃtikarmaṇi || 1 ||  
  
maṃtrārṇadvaṃdva madhyasthaṃ sādhyanāmākṣaraṃ likhet |  
vidarbha eṣa vijñeyo maṃtribhirvaśyakarmaṇi || 2 ||   
  
ādāvaṃte ca maṃtraḥ syānnyastosau saṃpuṭaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
eṣa saṃstaṃbhane śasta ityukto maṃtravedibhiḥ || 3 ||  
  
nāmna ādyaṃta madhyeṣu maṃtraḥ syādroṣano mataḥ |  
vidveṣaṇa vidhānena praśastamidamuttamaṃ || 4 ||  
  
maṃtrasyāṃte bhavennāma yogaḥ proccāṭane mataḥ || 5 ||   
  
aṃte nāmno bhavenmaṃtraḥ pallavo māraṇemataḥ || 6 ||   
  
sitaraktapītamiśra kṛṣṇadhūmrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
varṇato maṃtrataḥ proktā devatāḥ ṣaṭsukarmasu ||  
  
yaṃtrāṇāṃ lekhanaṃ dravyaṃ caṃdanaṃ rocanā niśā |  
gṛhadhūmavitāṃgārā māraṇeṣu viṣāṇi ca ||  
  
śyenāgni loṇapiṃḍāni dhattūrakarasastathā |  
gṛhadhūmastrikaṭukaṃ viṣāṣṭakamudīritaṃ ||  
  
devatā kālamudrādīn samyak jñātvā vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
ṣaṭkarmāṇi prayuṃjīta yathokta phalasiddhaye ||  
  
śyenaḥ syenaviṣṭhā | gṛhagodhikāgodhā | agniścitrakaṃ | loṇapiṃḍāni   
loṇamalaṃ | iti sarvavijānataḥ puruṣasya tattatkarmasiddhyati nānyatheti || jalādi   
bhūtodayo yathā |   
  
183a)  
  
ūrdhve vahniradhaścāpastiryak ketu prabhaṃjanaḥ | kṣomadhyapuṭe jñeyā nāmaḥ   
sarvatra pūritaṃ | iti vaśyādi karmaṇi svarodaya prāraṃbhe apekṣaṇīyaḥ || śāṃtau   
vaśye ca saumyāstithayaḥ | anyeṣu krūrāḥ | śāṃtivaśyayormṛdu   
dhruvanakṣatrāṇi | staṃbhane dhruvanakṣatrāṇi | māraṇādau ukta nakṣatrāṇi |   
śāṃtivaśyayoḥ saumyavārāḥ anyeṣu krūrāḥ | śāṃtivaśyastaṃbhaneṣu   
sthirāṇi lagnāni anyeṣu krūralagnāni | saumyakarmasu śubhasthānāni   
krūrakarmasutādṛśasthānāni | ityādayo'neke prakārāstattanmaṃtrajapādau   
voddhavyāḥ | iti maṃtrasaṃkṣepaḥ | etadvyatiriktānmaṃtrādi viśeṣān   
graṃthagauravānnalikhāmaḥ || bhosajjanāmamanatiḥ satataṃ bhavatsu kāryaṃ na   
jātu khalu sarvajanī name tat | vyaktī kṛtā yadihaguptatamāstumaṃtrāḥ   
saukaryatotra * * * * * * * ? || 1 ||   
  
yadgopitaṃ maṃtrasamūharatnaṃ sarvāgamajñairvividhāgameṣu |  
vyaktīkṛtaṃ tanmamamaṃtrakoṣe gṛhnaṃ tu lubdhvā sukhino bhavaṃtu || 2 ||  
  
śiṣṭo bhaṭṭasamāpa * * * * ? guṇa nidhirnaktya ca   
yovasthito nāmnaḥ premakarasya yo'janisutaḥ prītaḥ śivādityataḥ |   
āśādityamatīśvaraḥ sakṛtavān śrīratnamaṃtrāvalīkoṣaṃ koṣavataḥ sato   
bhavati kiṃdāridryabhītiḥ kṣitau || 3 || iti   
śrīmadāśādityatripāṭhīsaṃgṛhītemaṃtrakoṣemudrādikathanaṃ-  
  
१८४अ)  
  
आदर्शदोषान्मतिविभ्रमाद्वात्वराविशेषाल्लिखनस्यवेगात् ।   
यदत्र वृत्तं तदशुद्धवर्णं क्षमं तु संतः खलु लेखकस्य ॥ १ ॥   
  
भग्नपृष्ठकटिग्रीवस्तच्चदृष्टिरधोमुखः ।  
कष्टेन लिखितापुस्ती पुत्रवत् परिपालयेत् ॥ २ ॥  
  
पुस्तकलिखनपरिश्रमवेत्ता विद्वज्जनो नान्यः ।  
सारारलंघनखेदं हनूमानेकः परं वेद ॥ ३ ॥  
  
एतत् प्रयासं सकलं समीक्ष्य हरंति ये पुस्तकमस्मदीयं ।  
नेत्रस्य नाशंतन यस्य शोकं सर्वांगकुष्ठं लभतां स नित्यं ॥ ४ ॥  
  
श्रीशाके १५६५ पौषवदि १३ वुधानुराधायां लिखितं मनोहरसुत   
श्रीमदनंतरार्मणा ॥ शुभमस्तु ॥ विधः सर्वचराचरस्यदं च नेलब्धा   
प्रतिष्टात्वया सर्वं साधुमयं कृतं विरचितं चातुर्यहीनं द्वयं ।   
आम्रं साधुसुधारसं निरमितं स्थूलेन वीजेन किं निर्वीर्यौवनिता   
कुचौविरचितौ चेद् वेत्तयस्याषुतं ॥   
  
  
  
मुक्तबोद्ह इन्दोलोगिचल् रेसेअर्च्ह् इन्स्तितुते©२०११ मुक्तबोध इन्दोलोगिचल् रेसेअर्छ् इन्स्तितुते  अल्ल् रिघ्त्स् रेसेर्वेद्।ए-तेxत्स् मय् बे विएwएद् ओन्ल्य् ओन्लिने ओर् दोwन्लोअदेद् ड़ोर् प्रिवते स्तुद्य्।ए-तेxत्स् मय् नोत्, उन्देर् अन्य् चिर्चुम्स्तन्चेस्, बे चोपिएद्, रेपुब्लिस्हेद्,रेप्रोदुचेद्, दिस्त्रिबुतेद् ओर् सोल्द्, एइथेर् इन् ओरिगिनल् ओर् अल्तेरेद् ड़ोर्म्, wइथोउत्थे एxप्रेस्स् पेर्मिस्सिओन् ओड़् मुक्तबोध इन्दोलोगिचल् रेसेअर्छ् इन्स्तितुते इन् wरितिन्ग्।दत-एन्तेरेद् ब्य् थे स्तड़्ड़् ओड़् मुक्तबोध उन्देर् थे दिरेच्तिओन् ओड़् मर्क् स्। ग्। द्य्च्ज़्कोwस्कि।
